# Changelog

This changelog currently covers changes since **2025-11-21 09:00**. Entries are ordered newest first.

Each line is tagged with an approximate timestamp (`yyMMdd_HHmm`) and audience labels so both non-technical and technical readers can quickly see what changed and why.

## [0.4.50] — 2026-06-18 to 2026-06-24

### Changed
- [260622_2308] [User-facing] Settings: the Backup connections section moved below the AI provider section, with clearer copy on the custom-profile caveat. Commit dd072e4ef5. (Team Member)
- [260622_1925] [User-facing][Important] Mobile "Feedback & Bugs" is now durable by construction (260622_mobile-feedback-outbox) — the deferred mobile half of the 260622_feedback-bug-robustness desktop run. help.tsx no longer submits fire-and-forget; it **persists the report on-device through the existing generic OfflineQueue (Expo FileSystem) BEFORE the receipt**, fires an immediate `drain(isOnline)`, and retries on reconnect/foreground/periodic otherwise — surviving offline, flaky signal, and app background/kill. New `feedback` `QueueItemType` + bespoke `useFeedbackQueueConsumer` (submits via no-retry `submitFeedbackOnce` so the queue owns retry; classifies via the shared `classifyUploadFailureCategory`: 422→permanent/retained, 503/429/5xx→temporary, 401→auth, network→network). Honest status: a calm "Got it — your report is safe with Rebel, and on its way" receipt, a delivery-unavailable card (rendered off the permanent-failure flag, not a payload load) with a Copy-report fallback, and an honest "couldn't save" on QueueFullError. **Cloud-relay parity (the desktop Stage 3 gaps, closed for mobile):** a client-minted 32-hex `eventId` becomes the Sentry `event_id` via the scoped `scope.captureMessage(...,{event_id})` (retried reports dedup server-side, no duplicate issue), and a `clientReportId` drives per-report fingerprinting (each distinct report its own issue → Sentry→Linear fires per report). Both fields optional → backwards-compatible (web companion + older mobile unaffected). `request()` gained an optional `maxRetries` so `submitFeedbackOnce` reuses its header/capability/error logic. Reviewed cross-family (plan: native 82 / GPT 62; final: native 88 / GPT 82, all must-address resolved). Commits 0c43c191ea (cloud relay), e95cbc0733 (queue item + consumer), ace0aa6386 (offline-first help.tsx), e731f85f92 (Phase-7 fixes); rebel-system c888dba. (Team Member)
- [260621_2310] [User-facing][Important] Cloud-symlinked space indexing is now **ON by default** (260619_cloud-symlink-indexing S4–S5) — the final flip of the feature added flag-gated in the [260620_1200] entry below. A healthy cloud-backed Space (Google Drive / Dropbox / iCloud / OneDrive / Box reached via a workspace symlink) is indexed/searched like a local one without any opt-in; an explicit `experimental.cloudSymlinkIndexing === false` remains the kill-switch (and non-desktop surfaces, which have no fs executor, stay off). Two structural changes made this safe to default on: **(S4)** retired ~1050 LOC of "heavy machinery" — cloud is no longer LIVE-watched by chokidar at all (the dead-mount `lstat`/`readdir`-park hang class is gone by construction); the live-watch admission override, `restartCurrent` de-admission, the prober's decaying-backoff re-probe + recovery/degrade listener framing, `cloudRecoveryReindex.ts`, and the absence-purge producer are deleted, replaced by a single periodic re-walk scheduler (`cloudPeriodicRewalkService.ts`, 5-min `.unref()` tick: re-probe all cloud targets, re-walk when any is healthy) that re-joins a recovered space's content; the flap-debounced "Reconnecting" display verdict is preserved via a read-time settle. **(S5)** closed the last unbounded flag-ON paths — the bounded walker's readlink-first classifier no longer sync-`readlinkSync`s a nested symlink inside a containment-cloud space, and the `Glob`/`SearchFiles` tools route their root validation (and glob mtime fill) through the bounded workspace-fs boundary so a search rooted at a logical cloud-space path can't hang on a dead mount. Known v1 behaviour: content indexed while a space is healthy stays searchable after a flip-OFF unless query-time-gated. Cross-family reviewed (GPT-5.5-extra-high: the S4.2 deletion SHIP conf 90; the S5 fix+flip SAFE-TO-FLIP conf 90). Commits 8d9676efc4 / bc12d9f98e / 917a497468 (S4.1) · 9bb5c9fb64 (S4.3a) · 9285658923 / 31bcb2c19f (S4.2) · 03801ea7ad (S5). (Team Member)
- [260619_1150] [Developer-facing][User-facing][Open Source][Important] rebel-system is now MIT-licensed and public — Rebel's bundled skills, help docs, and agent instructions ship as a genuinely open-source submodule (history reseeded to an MIT root, `9807d9d`), and the old `-oss` mirror-substitution wiring that hid it is retired. The privacy policy is finalised at v3.2 (data controller: Mindstone Learning Limited), `CONTRIBUTING.md` adds public-repo data-hygiene rules (rebel-system + super-mcp), test/eval fixtures scrub real employee identifiers, and `mirror-publish` gains an inert opt-in OSS commit-marker trigger (plus a dry-run-only `skip_unit_tests` escape hatch). Commits 2e75fe9e3, 95ff6fa93, 40a8046eb, 009945419, e75738e23, dcee007d4, 362b54065; rebel-system 9807d9d / 6b09609 / e756b9b / b3b3daf / 6aa920c; super-mcp ca4fb65. (Team Member; Team Member)

### Added
- [260623_1334] [Developer-facing] Cloud indexing-coverage observability + prewarm consolidation — a follow-up to the cloud-Space indexing fix below. Adds a discovered-vs-admitted coverage gauge (so a "files exist on disk but never got admitted to the index" gap becomes visible rather than silent) and routes containment + sync-status checks through a single shared zero-I/O verdict-key source. Commits 4487a8c4ab, d539990e54, 55ac474468. (Team Member)
- [260623_0318] [User-facing][Important] The Mindstone managed subscription now works on mobile/cloud (260623_mobile-managed-subscription) — a turn run on Rebel's cloud (e.g. sent from the phone) can finally be served by a Mindstone-managed plan: the cloud serves the managed subscription (Layer 3a) and the desktop relays the managed key to the cloud on initial connect / syncNow (Layer 3b). Previously the cloud hard-coded managed-key availability to `false`, so `activeProvider:mindstone` users hit a terminal `missing-mindstone` route and got no response. Pairs with the mobile no-response fix in Fixed below. Commits f540a51177, 84cc2f1782, b247aa2b26, 9efa07c986; L3 cross-surface gate allowlist 72a214bf64. (Team Member)
- [260623_0817] [Developer-facing] Added `z-ai/glm-5.2` pricing to the knowledge-work eval catalogue so GLM 5.2 runs cost-account correctly in eval reports. Commits 05d5cf3f3a, 8d4ec1117a, 13b7b16833. (Team Member)
- [260623_0109] [Developer-facing] Terminal-route-decision telemetry — Rebel now emits a structured log (and a thresholded Sentry signal) when a turn reaches a terminal routing decision, giving observability into the managed-subscription / dialect-routing class of "why did this turn get no model". Commit 0ac6d53a1e. (Team Member)
- [260622_2151] [Developer-facing][Important] Native-teardown coverage contract + CI guard (260622_updater-teardown-lifecycle, Stages 1+4) — a structural class-kill for the macOS quit/update-hang family (5+ prior incidents). Every native owner that must be torn down on quit is now listed in a coverage manifest enforced by a CI guard, so a newly-added invisible native owner can't silently re-introduce the hang; plus a bounded moonshine ONNX dispose + fileIndex close on normal quit. The class invariant is enforced by an out-of-process watchdog rather than a JS coordinator (coordinator deferred). Commits 478026b115, 9a378c49d5, a488297ed3, 01964846d7, eefc309ac6, 5230210835. (Team Member)
- [260622_2132] [Developer-facing] Safety-eval billing-degradation guards (260622_safety-degradation-guards) — model-retry loops no longer retry non-transient errors (anti-regression for the earlier non-transient-retry fix), and `sentry-outcome-monitor` gains Check H, a sustained-rate degradation alert split by `reasonKind`. A 30-day backtest showed billing safety-eval degradation hitting ~6 distinct users/day, so the alert is framed as sustained-rate rather than spike. Commits 0832e443f3, 90b0416c7b. (Team Member)
- [260620_1200] [User-facing][Important] Healthy cloud-symlinked spaces are indexed/watched/searchable again, and a dead Drive can no longer freeze Rebel (260619_cloud-symlink-indexing). The 0.4.48→0.4.49 library-scan-freeze fix unconditionally excluded EVERY cloud-mount symlink target (Google Drive / Dropbox / iCloud / OneDrive / Box) from indexing, the Library tree, and the watcher — so healthy Drive spaces silently dropped out of search. This restores full admission for *healthy* spaces while making the hang class impossible by construction: a long-lived off-main-thread liveness **prober** (Electron `utilityProcess.fork` — separate OS process → its own libuv pool; per-probe timeout + kill-and-respawn in the parent; `worker_thread` ruled out by the Stage-0 spike as it shares the global pool and is un-killable when syscall-blocked) yields a cached, sync-readable per-space verdict (`healthy|degraded|unknown`). Admission of healthy spaces is gated behind `experimental.cloudSymlinkIndexing` (`LOCAL_ONLY_EXPERIMENTAL`, desktop-only; default-on flip is a separate owner/release decision). The "keep last-known index" contract: all index removals/existence-checks route through one **Removal Coordinator** (`src/main/services/indexRemovalCoordinator.ts`) with typed `RemovalReason`s and verdict-gating — not-`healthy`⇒RETAIN, branded `ReadlinkResolvedTarget`/`AbsenceProof` make "realpath a dead mount" and "purge on a `rootRealPath:null` walk" compile errors; search never `fs.access`-checks a cloud entry. A non-healthy space surfaces a per-space "Reconnecting" signal + last-known-results search notice and auto-recovers. Code spine: `src/core/services/cloudLivenessProbe{,.types}.ts`, `src/main/services/cloudLivenessProbeService.ts`, `src/main/workers/cloudLivenessWorker.ts`, `src/core/services/cloudSymlinkIndexing.ts` (`resolveSpaceSyncStatus`), `src/core/services/cloudSpaceContainment.ts`. Docs: [`docs/project/LIBRARY_SCAN_AND_CLOUD_WORKSPACES.md`](docs/project/LIBRARY_SCAN_AND_CLOUD_WORKSPACES.md), [the plan](docs/plans/260619_cloud-symlink-indexing/PLAN.md). (Team Member)

### Fixed
- [260624_0210] [User-facing][Important] Spaces whose backing folder was permanently deleted are now surfaced as a removable "can't find this folder" card instead of being silently dropped (260624_dead-space-surface-remove). A permanently-deleted folder/Drive leaves a dead symlink (link present, target gone): the scan caught the resulting `ENOENT` and **dropped** the candidate (so it was invisible in every UI list → un-removable) while `reconcileSpacesWithSettings`'s `lstat`-based existence check kept the stale `settings.spaces[]` entry (lstat succeeds on a dead link) and the scan re-probed it every ~5-min re-walk, emitting a recurring `warn` "Skipping inaccessible space candidate" (`code: ENOENT`). Root-cause fix at the scan catches in `_scanSpacesImpl` (`src/core/services/space/spaceService.ts`): a zero-I/O `error.code === 'ENOENT'` discriminator now pushes a degraded `SpaceInfo` (`status: 'needs_attention'`, `syncStatus: 'not_found'`, `sourcePath` preserved, `isSymlink: true`) via `buildDegradedSpace` instead of dropping it, and downgrades the per-scan warn. The `not_found` recovery UI (badge + Reconnect/Remove banner in `SpaceCard.tsx`) was already shipped — only a producer was missing. Removing the surfaced Space unlinks the dead symlink (cloud files untouched); the next reconcile then sees a real `lstat` ENOENT and prunes the settings entry through the existing path. No auto-delete of user config (option B rejected) and no behaviour change for healthy or temporarily-offline (`reconnecting`) cloud Spaces — the FS boundary siphons offline mounts to `reconnecting` before the catch. The classifier deliberately avoids a fresh readlink/stat so it can't re-introduce the cloud-mount main-thread-hang hazard. Cross-family reviewed (Cursor gpt-5.5 conf 87; Claude conf 88). Commits 9bd3fdf91c, 84ade81e70. (Team Member)
- [260623_1232] [Developer-facing][Open Source] OpenRouter OAuth now uses a localhost loopback redirect in dev and OSS builds, so the connect flow completes outside the packaged production scheme. Commit 637da18033. (Team Member)
- [260623_1206] [User-facing] The Library indexer handles much bigger and deeper folders — per-directory file cap raised 1,000→10,000 and max depth 12→15 — so large or deeply-nested Spaces index more completely (part of the cloud-Space indexing fix). Commit 6fa91077d2. (Team Member)
- [260623_1134] [Developer-facing] The proxy no longer logs the managed key's last-4 on the success-path passthrough log (privacy hardening). Commit a9daf0f06f. (Team Member)
- [260623_0930] [Developer-facing][Open Source][Important] OSS-build boot-crash hardening + a launch boot-smoke publish gate (260622_oss-toolindex-boot-crash, 260623_oss-boot-smoke-ci) — three startup-crash root causes in the open build are fixed by deferring eager module-load work to first access: `settingsStore` boot migrations (e2c4dc1033), `toolIndex` nativeRequire (521d26eb0c), and a redundant eager settings-listener bind that logged a boot stack trace (28774bafc8). A new launch-based OSS boot smoke (4d089ffcc8) now gates the public-mirror publish on Linux (6195bbe49f, 1229227f63, 19df0ecc00), so this class can't ship silently again. Also hardens the bundled meeting-bot commercial key (build-time inject via main-only env prefix + bundle guard + leak-gate patterns: 0392dfe831, 54695e94f8, 17c6634d1f, 658372c5fb). (Team Member)
- [260623_0715] [Developer-facing] Test/CI hardening sweep — mobile and `packages/shared` test files are now type-checked via dedicated ts-ratchet projects (they were checked nowhere, accumulating latent errors: ad66e609e5, 07f71e251d, 18c9784a59, 9674fb7916); a renderer poison-import graph guard kills the `@core/logger`→node-builtins renderer-bundle leak class by construction (a80a23670e, 61aca8b8f3); the `sk-*` drift scan skips vanished files to kill a TOCTOU self-test flake (642e11d1b9, c40cb58382); and three clobbered renderer import-bans were revived (32a8d931c3). Desktop boot-smoke is now a blocking publish gate on darwin for both channels (1f2d75b911). (Team Member)
- [260623_0334] [User-facing][Important] Mobile/web answers no longer regress after a reconnect (260623_render-drop-followups) — the mobile half of the desktop render-drop fix below. On reconnect, the cloud client's catch-up could wholesale-replace the live transcript with a stale per-conversation cache or a strict-shrink snapshot, dropping a just-finished answer. Now `fetchSession` applies the monotonic-content invariant at both the cache-hydrate and REST-replace sites: a replacement that would lower a shared turn's non-user message count or max event seq is refused, with an observable signal. Commits 164ddf75b3, 2eea0b1dd5, 9efa07c986, 7b9102c56d. (Team Member)
- [260623_0301] [User-facing][Important] Mobile "record → no response" / spurious "Original conversation deleted" fixed (260623_mobile-managed-subscription) — recording on mobile could silently produce no answer (and sometimes a false "Original conversation deleted"). Two causes: mobile treated a persisted `outcome:"error"` (and a missing persisted-ack from a current server) as success — including on the send-and-done recording path — and a managed-subscription turn couldn't be served on cloud (the Layer 3 work in Added). Now terminal-error and tombstone states surface as honest, recoverable failures, and a conversation is recreated only on a real tombstone, not on store-absence. Commits 863201b303, 14807a1493, 70f0505da7, 79bbcb2977, b049ac7d62. (Team Member)
- [260623_0158] [User-facing] GPT reasoning summaries no longer leak into the reply — when using GPT (Codex/Responses) models, the model's reasoning-summary text is routed to the dedicated thinking channel instead of appearing in the answer body, including for non-streaming Responses consumers. Commits b11bf48527, 1149999e52, 16a98dfee4, 79a22358d8. (Team Member)
- [260623_0139] [User-facing][Important] Packaged macOS file-watching is fixed — the idle-CPU storm and the disarmed quit-crash guard (260623_fsevents-nodepath-hoist) — the bundled file-watcher's eager `require('fsevents')` was hoisting ahead of the NODE_PATH shim in the packaged app, so it silently fell back to polling: ~2,800 stat-watchers burned a CPU core at idle and the quit-crash guard was disarmed. The shim is now hoisted first (extracted to `startup/initNodePath.ts`, with a source-order test), the poll interval is capped, and a non-silent warning fires if a packaged-darwin build ever falls back to polling again. Shipped to beta 0.4.4919417. Commits 7129477380, 296c7a2e54, 8140c4abec, ea8808f623, 640105e634. (Team Member)
- [260623_0103] [Developer-facing] Memory / behind-the-scenes turns no longer mis-route a non-servable model onto the Codex proxy (260622_memory-bts-route-mismatch) — both the codex route arm and the codex *profile* arm now gate on a shared `isCodexServableModel` predicate (with a native-Claude divert), backed by a client-seam backstop and a producer-granularity AST lint, so e.g. a `deepseek/*` behind-the-scenes model can't be sent onto the non-passthrough Anthropic transport and throw on the wire. Commits 04944d0b65, 033cbe5a12, 66b343d85f, 3337241fd9, c473d6004a. (Team Member)
- [260623_0040] [User-facing] Closing the last document tab now closes the preview drawer instead of reopening the document — the per-tab "X" on the only open document used to close it and immediately reopen it. Commit c605df8959. (Team Member)
- [260623_0018] [User-facing][Important] "Resolve file conflicts" false-positives fixed (Stage 1) (260623_conflict-dialog-false-positives) — the "you edited this on another device" conflict dialog was firing for AI memory files the user never touched (provenance-blind conflict detection × memory files that churn bytes every turn × multi-surface writes). Stage 1 ships honest, source-neutral copy (dialog and toast), pending-update compression, and orphan preservation. Stage 2 (lossless memory auto-merge) is deferred to let Stage 1 settle. Commits 7be09a6428, 00a08232dd. (Team Member)
- [260623_0100] [User-facing][Important] A completed turn's final answer can no longer vanish from the transcript after a background cloud sync (REBEL-6C0 / FOX-3524 + REBEL-6BZ / FOX-3523). Root cause: two layered defects — (1) **persistence**: `cloudRouter.ts` destructive else-branch full-replaced the local on-disk session with a cloud snapshot that was timestamp-newer but content-poorer on a shared turn (cloud's `updatedAt` could be bumped by a memory/activity push after the turn completed, making it chronologically newer but missing the final answer); (2) **renderer**: `ingestExternalSessions` wholesale-replaced the live in-memory transcript with no anti-regression guard, and the existing count-only guard was blind to the count-stable case (`mergeResultMessage` promotes an assistant message to `result` in-place — same id, same message count — so the final answer reverted to a preamble with a lower event seq but identical message count). Fix: (1) `localHasContentCloudLacks` (new predicate in `cloudRouterHelpers.ts`) returns true when, for any shared turn, local has more non-user messages OR a higher per-turn max valid event seq than cloud — routing those sessions through the already-safe additive `mergeSessionTurns` instead of the destructive full-replace; (2) `guardActiveIngestRegression` (new pure function in `src/core/services/sessionIngestGuard.ts`) refuses any external ingest that would shrink a shared turn's non-user message count or lower its max event seq, keeping the richer live transcript and emitting an observable breadcrumb. Critical correctness: `mergeEventsForDesktopPull` is intentionally local-wins-wholesale on shared terminal turns (see DELIBERATE ASYMMETRY comment in `sessionMergeUtils.ts` lines 277-288) — this asymmetry is what protects the local final answer and must not be symmetrized. Renderer import safety: the guard was extracted to a pure Node-free module after a cross-family reviewer caught a `@core/logger`→Node-builtins renderer-bundle hazard. Bug_mode + heavy CE2, 4 parallel diverse diagnosers (4-way convergence), cross-family GPT-5.5 review at each stage, red→green unit repros. Commits 81f8649d97, 460383b807 (Stage 1 persistence), 368af35a59, 36bac8511d (Stage 2 renderer guard). Plan: [`docs/plans/260622_fix-message-render-drop/PLAN.md`](docs/plans/260622_fix-message-render-drop/PLAN.md). (Team Member)
- [260622_1132] [User-facing][Important] A macOS auto-update that downloaded but wouldn't install no longer leaves the app stuck — when the relaunch-to-install handoff stalls, a watchdog now force-kills the lingering process (identity-guarded so it only ever targets Rebel's own bundle, never a same-PID stranger) so the in-place update completes instead of stranding the user on a force-quit. The force-kill signal and identity-guard outcome are recorded in the auto-update state store (`watchdogExternalForceKillSignal`, `watchdogExternalForceKillGuardOutcome`) for diagnosability. See [docs/plans/260622_mac-update-quit-force-kill/PLAN.md](docs/plans/260622_mac-update-quit-force-kill/PLAN.md). (Team Member)
- [260622_1130] [User-facing][Developer-facing][Important] "Feedback & Bugs" is robust by construction — the bug-report path no longer loses reports when the user's own LLM/provider/environment is broken, offline, or the app quits/crashes mid-send (the stated symptom: trusted users submitted via "Feedback & Bugs" but no `source:user-bug-report` appeared in Sentry). Root causes killed: (1) **capture-first / bounded-enrichment** — `bugReportHandlers.ts` mints a stable `report_id` + 32-char-hex `event_id` at entry, gathers all best-effort enrichment (Phase-A diagnostics, raw logs, the up-to-60s LLM analysis, update forensics) under **hard wall-clock deadlines**, then captures a SINGLE Sentry event with attachments assembled before capture (`scope.captureMessage(msg, level, {event_id})` — the only form that honors a preset id); the two previously-unbounded awaits (`exportRecentLogs`, `gatherUpdateForensics`) and the unbounded LLM total budget can no longer hang capture, and the `bugReportInFlight` guard self-heals via a monotonic generation token so a hung submit can't brick the feature for the session. (2) **Durable outbox** (`src/main/services/bugReportOutbox.ts`, NEW) — persist-before-`accepted` via atomic write + `fsync` + Windows-safe `.bak` replace, `.corrupt` quarantine, Zod-on-read with a per-record `schemaVersion` (deliberately NOT a `*STORE_VERSION` constant, to avoid a `DATA_SCHEMA_EPOCH` bump), byte caps, delete-only-on-confirmed-2xx, backoff-with-jitter, drain wakes (immediate / boot dir-scan / backoff-timer / `powerMonitor.resume` / `will-quit` drain alongside the asset/content outboxes), circuit breaker honoring `Retry-After`, and a dead-letter that emits its **own** Sentry event (a silent local dead-letter would be reborn-invisible — the exact bug). (3) **`beforeSend` exemption** (`src/main/sentry.ts`) — events tagged `source: 'user-bug-report'` skip the message-content drops, so a user pasting a backend error (`Failed query: insert into "rebel"`) is never silently filtered. (4) **Fingerprint entropy** — `setFingerprint(['user-bug-report', title, report_id])` so each submission is its own issue and the external Sentry→Linear automation fires per report (closes the confirmed `'harry test'` ×2 → single REBEL-692 collapse); legitimate deviation from `sentry-fingerprint-for-structured-errors` (bug reports use `captureMessage` outside the `KNOWN_CONDITIONS` registry). (5) **Honest status** (`src/renderer/src/bugReportToastCopy.ts`, `src/shared/ipc/channels/bugReport.ts`) — `queued|delivered|delivery-unavailable|failed`; one "Got it" toast on durable write, `delivered` is a silent upgrade (never a fake "sent" on a non-confirming transport 2xx), `delivery-unavailable` is a warning with a Copy-report + Rebels-community fallback, boot-time unsolicited toasts suppressed. (6) **Cross-surface + observability** — cloud (`cloud-service/src/routes/feedback.ts`, `sentryFeedback.ts`) stops dishonest-success: returns **503 FEEDBACK_FAILED** when Sentry is unconfigured / `flush()` returns false (transport timeout), and a **non-transient 422** for known-permanent config failures (so the cloud-client doesn't retry a hopeless request); `scripts/sentry-outcome-monitor.mjs` gains **Check G** reconciling PostHog `Bug Report Submitted` counts vs `source:user-bug-report` Sentry volume (the standing detector that would have surfaced this class months earlier). Mobile offline-queue durability deferred-with-ticket. Bug_mode + Heavy CE2, cross-family reviewed (GPT-5.5-extra-high + native Claude), red→green durability/liveness repros. Commits 5f602f9a4c, cd86a7bb06, b255ef12fe, 69392b1b22, 089a707c02, 6ca5ac0602, aa9332058b, 86647c5543, 797fa33b31. Plan + Intent & Design Rationale: [`docs/plans/260622_feedback-bug-robustness/PLAN.md`](docs/plans/260622_feedback-bug-robustness/PLAN.md). (Team Member)
- [260622_1010] [User-facing][Important] Approved tool actions that fail ARGUMENT VALIDATION no longer show users a raw, jargon-filled red toast (FOX-3519; REBEL-6BM + ~15 consolidated, previously-Canceled per-tool `[Autopilot]` tickets). When a staged/approved `use_tool` call failed validation — the super-mcp wrapper (`ARG_VALIDATION_FAILED`: `use_tool "args" must be an object …`), the per-tool validator (`-33003 Argument validation failed …`), or the downstream-MCP validator (`Downstream validation failed …`) — the renderer classified it `execution-failed` and surfaced the raw validator body, **including agent-directed guidance** ("Use `get_tool_details` / `dry_run: true` / `search_tools`"), as an alarming "Approved, but the action failed: …" error toast to our non-technical audience. The agent already self-recovers from this class via its parallel failure-notice continuation. Now `classifyStagedError` routes the class to a new `arg-recovering` outcome → a calm `info` toast ("Rebel is sorting that out") while the agent retries; the **exhausted-retries** terminal case (super-mcp appends "Arguments may require user clarification" after `STOP_RETRYING_THRESHOLD`) routes to a distinct `arg-needs-detail` `warning` toast ("Rebel needs a bit more from you") so the user isn't falsely reassured. Genuine non-arg execution failures (timeout/auth/network/backend) keep their red `execution-failed` toast; the safety/approval gate is unchanged (this only changes how a POST-approval failure is surfaced/recovered). Detection (`isArgValidationFailure`) keys on the stable validator substrings + the `-33003`/`ARG_VALIDATION_FAILED` code markers so future wording drift still classifies. Also a Sentry fingerprint groups any residual arg-validation error toast into one issue (`['toast','tool-arg-validation-failed']`) instead of N per-tool singletons. Desktop-renderer-only by construction — cloud/mobile never surfaced the raw validator error (MCP `isError` resolves without throwing). Chief-designer-approved copy; cross-family reviewed (GPT-5.5-extra-high, conf 89, 2 must-fix addressed) + red-green tested. Follow-ups: structural staging-time hardening of `extractMcpPayload`, the cloud/mobile silent-drop on `{success:false}`, and the narrow `rebel_browser_*` staged-vs-direct parity gap (FOX-3519 notes). **Refinement (commit `b0d073ff3f`):** both toasts now NAME the action ("…the details for **Send email**…") via the staged item's humanized display name (`buildToolDisplayName`, already shown on the approval card — not the validator string), with a graceful generic fallback when the name is absent. Agent-voiced "which field is missing" specifics were deliberately NOT added — the only per-field signal is the forbidden validator jargon. Cross-family reviewed again (GPT-5.5-extra-high, SHIP WITH NITS, conf 87, no must-fix). Commits aa9ad4790b, 6a9ba39668 + b0d073ff3f. (Team Member)
- [260621_0445] [User-facing][Developer-facing][Important] Connection failures are no longer mislabeled as "the AI provider had a moment" (REBEL-6B6 / FOX-3513, diagnosability) — when the real cause is a client-side transport failure (a VPN, firewall, proxy, captive portal, or plain offline blocking the AI host), Rebel was wrapping the `fetch failed` / connect-timeout as a generic `server_error`, which both misled the user *and* erased the discriminating signal so the class couldn't be sized fleet-wide. A new discriminated `network` error kind now flows from the classifier (`modelErrors.ts`, minted only from allowlisted network errnos / `fetch failed` via `isNetworkError()` over message + `error.cause.code` — a genuine provider 5xx stays `server_error`) through to calm user copy ("Can't reach the AI service… usually a connection issue on this device") that points to the existing "Check AI services" diagnostic instead of a useless provider switch, plus a "ChatGPT Pro uses a different host than the OpenAI API" clarifier in the reachability panel. The class is now countable via `ai_error_shown.errorKind=network` + Sentry `model_error.kind=network`. Recovery is unchanged (network still gets longer backoff, no provider-switch); the bypass is now keyed on the authoritative error *kind* (string-match only as a fallback for un-classified errors), which also stops a real 5xx whose body happens to contain "fetch failed" from being misrouted as a network problem. Cross-family reviewed (GPT-5.5 + Claude) + red-green tested. (Team Member)
- [260619_2351] [User-facing][Important] PDF preview in the document editor no longer renders as a blank grey panel in the packaged app — a `blob:` URL minted inside the packaged `file://` renderer can't be fetched by Chromium's out-of-process PDF viewer, so PDFs are now streamed over the privileged `rebel-media://` protocol (the proven video/audio path), which is origin-independent. An always-visible "Open in default app" affordance means a blank preview can never strand you. Commit b357480951. (Team Member)
- [260619_2333] [User-facing][Important] Conversation search in the sidebar is materially more trustworthy (7 fixes) — exact keyword and title matches now survive the semantic-similarity floor (opt-in lexical-exemption keep-rule; auto-context retrieval stays strict), the "Last 24h / 7 / 30 days" chip scopes the actual search (quick **and** "search all messages") instead of trimming a few results after the fact, renamed conversations are re-embedded so they're findable by the new title, short / proper-noun queries get an instant title-substring fallback, automation conversations are indexed for the Automations filter, and the UI distinguishes "search is warming / temporarily unavailable" from a genuine no-match (never implying your conversations are gone). Commits eaedb5367, fb744ec50, 4ca767522, f5836f8b8, e07247842, 6949a0a19, fa9cd9d68, 0a9be0a36; rebel-system 976819b. (Team Member)
- [260619_2239] [User-facing] Find Similar results now have a visible way out — a "Back to all conversations" header and a working ESC key (the mode was previously tracked only by a non-reactive ref, so the exit controls never appeared), plus a guard against out-of-order re-triggers that could leave the panel stuck or flashing stale results. Commits 609d6e336, f5ba31e18, 6c161d6be. (Team Member)
- [260619_2212] [User-facing][Important] "I sent a prompt and nothing came back" turn wedges are hardened — a turn that stalls *before* the model request is even dispatched (e.g. when the libuv thread pool is saturated by cloud-mount symlink walking) now errors-and-retries instead of spinning silently, via an attempt-scoped idempotency guard and a live-attempt-epoch registry (closed by construction). The thread-pool floor is raised and cloud-root validation bounded (Stage 4b), the file-watcher's cloud-symlink exclusion resists nested/dead mounts (Stage 4a), and the wedge now emits an alertable terminalKind plus a support-facing "all providers unreachable" verdict in the diagnostics bundle. Commits e04d2b308, 6eaddbe9f, 4a71b59f6, 17520c67b, 0c4b052f6, 532e32518, b9316ff70, 6b4402d18. (Team Member)
- [260619_1805] [User-facing] Connector tool calls fail less often because the model used the wrong invocation pattern (REBEL-61S) — when the model calls a package tool by its bare name, it's now guided through the `get_tool_details` → `use_tool` discovery flow instead of erroring with "Unknown tool", reinforced by a matching rebel-system system-prompt clarification. Commits c1099a2ef, 736f1a1be; rebel-system b3b3daf. (Team Member)
- [260619_1349] [User-facing] Rebel handles a busy or full machine more gracefully — it raises the open-files limit at startup and bounds the top file-descriptor-exhaustion (EMFILE) sites, and surfaces a calm "disk is full" warning toast on ENOSPC instead of failing mysteriously. Cloud-storage detection also broadens to catch Dropbox / OneDrive File Provider mounts (not just Google Drive / iCloud). Commits 21487930a, e5c355e05, c7385c5b0, b8403adad. (Team Member)
- [260619_1341] [User-facing] First-run onboarding feels smoother — `useConnectorSetupGuidance` is memoised to kill a render-churn loop in the connector-setup step. Commit 8518d82c8. (Team Member)
- [260619_1155] [User-facing] The What's New sidebar card is easier to read — the "Try it" hover pill moved off the title row so it no longer covers the (i) tooltip, the tooltip copy is honest, and long titles clamp to two lines. Commits 5eec904c6, 59b452077. (Team Member)
- [260619_1149] [User-facing] Memory-update status survives cloud catch-up — cross-surface memory-update status is now persisted (closing a gap where a status set on one device didn't reach another) and broadcast to live UI before the disk write, so the indicator isn't blocked on a slow save. Commits c8fc450ed, a59559ce5, df0ec6dae. (Team Member)
- [260619_1130] [User-facing][Important] Cloud-storage sync-conflict duplication loop killed at the generator (REBEL-696 / FOX-3498, recurrence #3) — for Spaces whose files live inside a cloud-storage mount (Google Drive / Dropbox / iCloud / OneDrive / Box, detected via `resolveWorkspaceWriteAuthority === 'desktop_fs_authoritative'`, incl. through Rebel's per-Space workspace symlinks), the desktop cloud-sync pull no longer writes EXISTING files in place. Previously both the OS sync engine AND Fly cloud-sync wrote the same paths (two writers, no cross-machine authority), which is what the OS engine mints `(1)` conflict copies from — and they could self-feed. Now `cloudWorkspaceSync` defers `reason:'edited'` pulls indefinitely on cloud-authoritative paths (the OS engine owns delivering cross-device edits), keeps the `reason:'new'` force-delivery lifeline for genuinely cloud-only-origin files but via atomic temp-then-rename (non-racing, EXDEV-safe), and gates the `.conflict-cloud` in-place writer (quarantines to a local non-synced location + broadcasts instead of dropping a file into the synced subtree). `cloudStagingBridge.pullPublishedFileFromCloud` is handled as a force-delivery sibling for parity. PUSH (upload) is unchanged, so phone/web read continuity is preserved. A mobile/web edit to an existing cloud-backed file (which the OS engine can't deliver to the desktop) is recorded as a hash-keyed pending cloud update and surfaced in `WorkspaceConflictDialog` as a one-click "Newer version available — Update to newest" (distinct from a 3-way conflict; no silent staleness). Auto-applies on update; the prior conflict pile still needs a one-time cleanup. Detection-general, behaviour-confirmed where spiked (Google Drive + iCloud spiked live 2026-06-19; Dropbox detection-covered; OneDrive/Box detection-covered, not behaviourally spiked). Supersedes the exhausted suppression-matcher fix-class from the two prior recurrences. (Team Member)
- [260619_1100] [User-facing][Important] A relocated macOS app no longer bricks an auto-update — the updater prevents the app bundle from being moved mid-install and fails loudly on an install error instead of leaving a broken half-installed app (a root cause of the bricked-beta incident), with an integration smoke test over the move flow. Commits 008189200, a44e7def1. (Team Member)

### Developer-facing & Infrastructure
- [260619_2333] [Developer-facing][Important] The automated-boot-hang class is killed by construction — startup native dialogs (the macOS app-relocation / duplicate-bundle `NSAlert`s that wedged packaged E2E and `package:run` dev boots) now route through a single headless/automated-context SSOT (`isHeadlessCli`) and are skipped in test/headless mode, enforced by new ESLint `no-raw-startup-dialog` + `no-raw-headless-check` rules. ~10 ad-hoc headless/test-mode checks were consolidated onto the SSOT (the dead "switch belt" dropped). Commits edd9e08a5, 6af84a23c, f1fa1decf. (Team Member)
- [260619_2253] [Developer-facing] Custom-gateway Gemini `thought_signature` handling is hardened beyond the 260618 auto-incompatible marking — a PII-safe gateway diagnostic (counts only; the signature value is never emitted), streaming signature flags preserved across delta reordering, and fail-open behaviour so a reorder glitch can't break the turn. Commits 5c94a24d8, 5f117fce5. (Team Member)
- [260619_2238] [Developer-facing] The pre-push / `validate:fast` gate is faster and harder to rot — the bts-prefix-decoder self-test runs against a minimal ESLint config (2.2 GB → 0.3 GB, 5.4 s → 0.6 s), knip runs concurrently with vitest at push time, `[deploy-beta]`-style commit markers are detected from the subject line only (with an anti-rot guard), a stacked dual-retry anti-pattern in `clientFactory` is guarded, and knip-health is reconciled. Commits f1323765c, 7f134cc78, f0ddc7df9, 3b29af6b9, 063b3266d, 77557df7c, d3c1e12e0. (Team Member)
- [260619_2212] [Developer-facing][Important] Production promotion is becoming CI-driven — a promote pre-flight verdict library (Stage 1), a CI-triggered promote command + driver (Stage 2), a `test:realboot` boot check wired on both channels (Stage 3, currently observe-first — not yet blocking publish), and self-maintaining changelog version headings (S10). The release Sentry Outcome Monitor is also hardened with a dedicated `SENTRY_MONITOR_AUTH_TOKEN` and self-diagnosing 403 classification. Commits 3785af316, ed6ad46b6, 12e64bb1e, 51f8029ff, 96440dac5, 7481a4c6c. (Team Member; Team Member)
- [260619_1901] [Developer-facing] Multi-provider routing foundation (Stages 4b–7) lands behind the default-off `experimental.multiProviderRoutingEnabled` flag and is inert in production — rate-limit failover with observability, Codex→Claude divert correctness (F1), and a flag-gated Settings "Backup connections" UI (hidden unless the flag is on) with an `activeProvider`↔`enabledProviders` write contract and search-index registration. No user-visible behaviour change until the flag is flipped. Commits 04afd64d7, f174c1de0, bbb617dab, d68fde07c, 1301cd1c4. (Team Member)
- [260619_1513] [Developer-facing] New turn-observability thin slice — one PII-safe `Agent Turn Terminal Observed` event per turn (origin / provider / duration / terminalKind / app-retry-count / offline-detected) emitted from turn cleanup, decoupled from registry/partial-mock fragility. Observability-only, fail-open. Commits 80a4bdb6e, 96a3bbcd3. (Team Member)
- [260619_1211] [Developer-facing] Sentry noise reduction — a self-referential logger that can't write to disk (ENOSPC/EMFILE) no longer emits a second Sentry event about the failed write (REBEL-15G/660/69M), and transient MCP config-read failures classify as warnings rather than failing the health check (REBEL-ZF). Commits 8c19e9f49, 0ef5f80ee. (Team Member)

## [0.4.49] — 2026-06-16 to 2026-06-18

### Changed
- [260618_2255] [User-facing] Calmer "working" indicator — while Rebel is working, the live progress area now shows one thing at a time (the concrete current activity) instead of stacking several signals. The witty persona quips are demoted to fill genuine silence or re-engage on a long wait (static >25s), rather than rotating over real progress; elapsed time stays visible but quiet, and exactly one live region is announced to screen readers. Past versions of this area felt distracting and noisy — this keeps it calm without losing capability (sub-agent detail still reachable via Technical details). (`show-more-activity` Stage 4; commit ba46199aa) (Team Member)
- [260618_1850] [User-facing][Important] A model reached through a custom gateway that hits the Gemini `thought_signature` tool-call error is now auto-marked tool-use-incompatible on its profile — Rebel stops re-attempting the same failing tool call every turn (and degrades gracefully) instead of erroring identically each time, with the affected-gateway reasoning suppression validated end-to-end. Commits 9fa311967, 8d62bc3f0. (Team Member)
- [260618_1550] [User-facing] Background and automation runs no longer masquerade as Active conversations (REBEL-6A3) — app-initiated sessions (automations, behind-the-scenes work) were leaking into the Active list, the pinned-tabs strip, unread/home/mobile send controls, and could leave hidden "active ghosts" when starred. They're now excluded by construction via session *kind* (not origin), so only conversations you actually started appear as Active. Commits c57ff4ca1, aa20d9f78, 29e226aba, 9c76a311c, 92803bfd7, 6fbd0c760, a1697bf74. (Team Member)
- [260618_1300] [Developer-facing][Important] Removed the manual `ModelProfile.reasoningDisabled` ("Off" thinking) flag (REBEL-5RJ) — thinking suppression for incompatible custom gateways is now driven **solely** by the auto-detected `thinkingCompatibility` verdict via a single shared gate (`shouldSuppressProfileReasoning` in `@shared/utils/reasoningSuppression`, re-exported from `modelLimits`), consumed by the direct client (incl. Codex mode), the desktop proxy + Codex inheritance seam, the planner routing catalogue, and the read-only thinking display. `normalizeSettings` migrates legacy `reasoningDisabled:true` profiles → `thinkingCompatibility:'incompatible'` (drops the key, clears effort) so their suppression survives rather than re-leaking `reasoning_effort`. The wizard's Thinking-level "Off" segment is removed. Rebel deliberately does not offer a turn-thinking-off-by-choice preference. (Team Member)
- [260617_1410] [User-facing] Claude Fable 5 is hidden from model-selection surfaces while access is withdrawn, so you can't pick a model Rebel can't currently serve. Defaults are unchanged. Commit d54867f2c. (Team Member)
- [260616_2230] [Developer-facing][Open Source][Important] OSS license framework switched to **Business Source License 1.1 + DCO** — adopting Josh's `rebel-license-bundle`, which supersedes the earlier (never-signed-off) bespoke MSL-1.0 + CLA suite. Same commercial substance (100-Installed-Seat Additional Use Grant, each version converting to MIT on its 2-year Change Date) but a standard, widely-recognised license. Contributors now sign off with the **Developer Certificate of Origin** (`git commit -s`) plus a one-line inbound sublicensing grant in `CONTRIBUTING.md` — **no CLA**. Root `LICENSE`/`NOTICE`/`README`/`TRADEMARK`/`CODE_OF_CONDUCT` reconciled, entity standardised to "Mindstone Learning Limited", `package.json` license → `BUSL-1.1`, `CLA.md`/`CCLA.md` removed, `DCO.txt`/`LICENSING.md`/`COMMERCIAL.md` added, and the mirror header machinery made BSL-1.1-aware (per-file header text locked; bake deferred). Per-file header rollout and submodule MIT flips (`mcp-servers`, skills) are tracked follow-ups; residual BSL drafting/relicensing reads are with legal. (Team Member)

### Added
- [260618_2250] [User-facing][Important] Rebel now shows a bit more of what it did — finished messages carry a calm one-line recap of the turn. It's an AI-written sentence (e.g. "Pulled your Q3 numbers from Slack and drafted the update"), generated on the cheap behind-the-scenes Haiku model and grounded *strictly* in the turn's real activity (no fabrication — eval-gated with a deterministic no-fabrication hard gate, `evals/activity-summary.ts`). Persisted per-turn (`AgentSession.activitySummaryByTurn`, no store-version bump), merged across desktop↔cloud sync via `unionPerTurnMap` so it survives reconciliation, and live-swapped in via a new `session:activity-summary-generated` broadcast. When the sentence isn't available (failed/slow/old turn, or a turn without enough tool work) it falls back to a deterministic count-line — "3 files · 12 tools · 1m 20s" (`deriveTurnActivityRecap`). Surfaces on ordinary completed turns (the `ContextualProgressCard` collapsed label) and on primary-MCP-app turns (the work disclosure). Generated only for substantial turns (≥2 tools or ≥1 file). Motivation: surface a bit more of what Rebel does so the felt experience is "look at all it did" rather than "why so long". (`show-more-activity` CE2 run; commits 08a48d6c3 / 3a7d07ffc / e3ff7b49d / 2730c24ee / da6877f28) (Team Member)
- [260618_1940] [User-facing][Open Source] Tool calls with slightly malformed arguments are now auto-repaired from the tool's own schema instead of failing outright — super-mcp 2.6.0 adds schema-driven `use_tool` argument auto-repair at the router, with app-side success-based hydration, a default-off enforcing mode (`REBEL_ENFORCE_SCHEMA_GATE`), a canonical hydration key, and compile-enforced stream-event classification so repaired calls hydrate reliably. super-mcp's source is public. Commits 94b02ad (super-mcp), 780a60040, 9adbb5091, 45032b3e5, fe34cc745. (Team Member)
- [260618_1440] [User-facing][Open Source] One-click meeting-recorder setup in the open build — Settings → Meetings now has a "Set up recorder" button that installs Recall's Desktop SDK for you, instead of asking you to copy an `npm install` line into a terminal and restart by hand. The dialog walks through install → progress ("up to a minute", cancellable) → a "Restart Rebel" prompt, surfaces a plain-language error with a retry (and an honest "macOS/Windows only" note where Recall ships no build), and keeps the copy-the-command path as a fallback. The recorder stays opt-in and default-missing: the install uses `--no-save`, so `package.json` (and the public-mirror dependency strip) is untouched, and the affordance is still gated purely on the SDK not resolving at runtime — no build-flavor flag. New desktop-only IPC (`meeting-bot:install-recorder` / `:cancel-recorder-install` / `:is-recorder-installing`), reusing the existing cross-platform npm runner and `app:relaunch`. Success requires npm-OK **and** the native recorder binary actually present — a partial/failed install is cleaned up so it can't get stuck "installed-but-broken". (Team Member)
- [260618_0010] [User-facing][Important] Rebel tells you when it's waiting too long on a model (and lets you act) — if a turn sits waiting on the model with nothing coming back, instead of an indefinite "thinking" spinner you now see a calm "still on this one — taking longer than usual" note with inline **Try again** / **Stop** after ~30s. It only appears before the first word arrives (a normal, slowly-streaming answer stays "thinking"), never nags a healthy turn, and "Try again" cleanly stops-and-resends rather than firing a second request. Interactive turns only (automation is unaffected). Commit 87bdcc9fb. (Team Member)

### Fixed
- [260618_2045] [User-facing] Workspace health checks stop crying "critical" on a flaky network or an iCloud Documents workspace — the access-probe wrapper/retry timeout race is fixed, iCloud Documents folders are detected, the whole health call (including cleanup) runs under one overall deadline, the abort path no longer leaks a file handle, and cold xattr reads are skipped on known-cloud paths. Part of an iCloud/flaky-network degradation investigation. Commits 721883bf5, df0951bae, f5ad999bf, ae18f4b35, 1916babbd. (Team Member)
- [260618_1930] [User-facing] Search no longer claims you have zero matches when the index is actually unavailable — semantic search, `rebel_search_sources`, and `rebel_search_files` now distinguish "search is temporarily unavailable" from a genuine empty result (via `semanticSearchWithStatus`), FTS-index degradation is surfaced via a Sentry known-condition with an honest health warning, and the semantic-index health copy stays honest when the index isn't open. Commits b9e1bb7b6, d69ddba6d, fad26b938, a921de740, 28bc95505. (Team Member)
- [260618_1900] [User-facing][Important] Conversation transcript rendering is more trustworthy — staged-tool failure notices no longer render as editable "you" messages, double-materialized duplicate result messages collapse on hydration, and a silent cloud-merge that clears a locally-Done conversation now emits observable "resurrection" telemetry instead of a mystery reappearance. Commits 1d434a5fe, b90a17113, e7654ce02. (Team Member)
- [260618_1830] [User-facing][Important] Session-index writes and quit-time saves no longer race or drop work — the global session `index.lock` is serialized in-process to close a cross-session dropped-write (with slow-wait telemetry), the quit-time sync save defers behind in-flight async writers to avoid lock contention, and a single `hydrateSession()` boundary plus a by-construction guard closes the raw-parse class. Commits a7aea6fad, d2468897f, 628e34a1d, 41f12c797, 777519761, b7501fbcd, 1cd3b1916. (Team Member)
- [260618_1800] [User-facing][Important] Store migrations are non-destructive across desktop and cloud, more conversation history is kept, and resolved automations stay done — the migration machinery is hardened across all 12 `migrateStore` callers so a version bump can't wipe data, `MAX_PERSISTED_SESSIONS` rises 10k→25k, and `doneAt` is backfilled for resolved automations that an index rebuild had reverted to Active. Commits 59d8a0144, 26825ac8d, 3ac99909f, 6548cecd6. (Team Member)
- [260618_1700] [User-facing] Onboarding is quieter and more honest when something goes wrong — shipped debug `console.warn` spam is removed from the onboarding wizard, and best-effort onboarding catches are now observable (`ignoreBestEffortCleanup`) instead of silently swallowed. Commits 701e61a48, bf9e75d29. (Team Member)
- [260618_1655] [User-facing][Important] The Library no longer hangs forever scanning Google Drive / iCloud / OneDrive workspaces — the file scan stopped following symlinks into cloud mounts (generalised into a shared `safeWalkDirectory` choke-point), is Windows UNC/device-namespace-robust, redacts PII in symlink telemetry, and lets backup/snapshot collectors opt out of the skip. Distinct root cause from the already-shipped Bug-2 file-tree memory bound; no data loss. Commits b25ccb4f0, b98ff6905, 3d6d091a6, 298d6eea4, b527b6aa6, 967a5e1a6, bb9beadbf. (Team Member)
- [260618_0210] [User-facing][Important] "I sent a prompt and nothing came back" no longer leaves you stuck forever — an interactive turn that stalls waiting on the model (request sent, no response streaming) now ends after a conservative 5 minutes (was up to 10) as a clean **"That took too long — Try again"**, instead of a frozen spinner. Reliable on both the normal and the abrupt-abort code paths. Commit 606acba59. (Team Member)
- [260617_2240] [User-facing][Important] Downloading diagnostics can no longer hang on "Preparing…" — on a busy/large machine the diagnostic-bundle export could spin forever (which also blocked us from helping when something went wrong). Each part of the bundle now has a time limit, the export always finishes (telling you honestly if a section had to be skipped), there's an always-works minimal fallback, and the Settings → Diagnostics download got the same protection. Commits 41ef49b5a + the Stage-2 set. (Team Member)
- [260617_1840] [User-facing] A single calendar-sync blip no longer triggers "Calendar Cache needs attention" — a shared consecutive-failure streak withholds failure-class issues until they're sustained (≥2 syncs), and network-shaped errors get honest "couldn't reach your calendar, retrying" copy instead of blaming your connection. Commits 6d540343a, dc412e5d6. (Team Member)
- [260617_1530] [User-facing][Important] Outbound network calls are more reliable under load — DNS resolution is decoupled from libuv's 4-thread pool (cacheable c-ares lookup with fallback) to fix a starvation that could stall everything from model calls to meeting captures; meeting-bot transcript-save retries are bounded (no more retry storm when attempts weren't incrementing) with terminal-failed audit/retry telemetry; and the Codex proxy retries once on a pre-response network blip. Commits fb7f72095, 11af92d47, 8ab655bdc, 5d072a900. (Team Member)
- [260617_0447] [User-facing][Important] A single malformed session can no longer crash `sessions:list`, hide your conversations, or break every turn — `classifySessionKind(undefined)` no longer throws, and transient index-read failures no longer hide data that should be visible. Commits 54840aec3, 7f8a58acc. (Team Member)
