- [260618_1650] [Developer-facing][Open Source] Public-mirror leak-gate hardening — strips the Elastic-2.0 `@rudderstack/analytics-js` dependency from the mirror, relocates the leak-gate tooling under `mirror/` (closing a private-name leak), scrubs all non-Mindstone emails and extends private-name scrubbing (with `CONTRIBUTORS.md` exempt), and keeps `docs/reports` public as build-critical, non-leak material. Commits b77fbf85f, d294de624, 9f417c3f7, 4fc82657b, 1e3a15f6d, 7d7cb3081. (Team Member; Team Member)
- [260618_0210] [Developer-facing][Important] Self-diagnosing telemetry for stalls + an observable quit-deadlock — the `awaiting_api` watchdog-stall capture now records time-to-first-token, first-byte-received, provider/route, and a cheap stall-gated network-reachability marker (so a "nothing came back" stall reveals whether the provider call ever connected — pinpoints the DNS-threadpool class). Adds a bounded `quit_deadlock_detected` diagnostic event (ledger-first, then a bounded Sentry flush so it can't itself hang the quit) from the macOS install fallbacks + graceful-shutdown race, plus a **bounded force-exit fallback on the Windows install path** (which had none) so an Electron ≥41 quit-deadlock is no longer telemetry-blind — it fires only on a genuine hang, never on a normal install. Commit cb1d364a9. (Team Member)
- [260617_2113] [Developer-facing][Important] SSRF DNS-rebinding TOCTOU closed — each outbound request now uses a per-request undici dispatcher pinned to the already-validated IP, discarded response bodies are cancelled so pinned dispatchers release their sockets, and dispatcher close is guaranteed even if the body cancel rejects. Commits 9b577d337, 4e682e3d1, 795fd53df, d31d30e20. (Team Member)

## [0.4.48] — 2026-06-15 to 2026-06-16

### Added
- [260616_2212→260618] [User-facing] Gateway thinking-compatibility handling (REBEL-5RJ) — a model served through a custom gateway that mistranslates `reasoning_effort` into a thinking format the model rejects (e.g. a litellm→Vertex proxy emitting legacy `thinking.type:"enabled"` for a model that requires adaptive) is handled by **auto-detection**: the profile **Test** button records `thinkingCompatibility:'incompatible'`, and every profile-driven egress path then omits `reasoning_effort` for that profile (self-healing if a later Test succeeds). **NOTE:** the originally-implemented manual "Off" toggle (`ModelProfile.reasoningDisabled`, commit 4cb68fc13) was **superseded and removed before release** (2026-06-18) — see the `[Unreleased]` Changed entry — in favour of this single auto-detected signal. Rebel does not offer a manual turn-thinking-off control. Additive; no IPC contract change. (Team Member; revised 2026-06-18)

### Fixed
- [260616_2212] [User-facing] Real gateway error reason surfaced + one-click serving-profile recovery (REBEL-5RJ) — when a provider/gateway returns an actionable 400 (e.g. a litellm→Vertex proxy "thinking.type.enabled is not supported; use thinking.type.adaptive"), the banner previously showed generic "Something went sideways"/"AI rejected the request" copy. `extractHttpErrorMessage` now recovers the embedded provider message from wrapped non-JSON bodies and `classifyErrorUx` surfaces it (redacted, via the dispatcher's clean `ModelError.message`) on the invalid_request banner. Separately, when a recoverable "model can't run on the active provider" terminal fires and a credential-reachable selectable profile serves that exact model, the recovery banner leads with "Use <profile>" (switch-model to `profile:<id>`) and the IPC handler resolves the ref and pins `workingProfileId`/`thinkingProfileId` so the turn routes through that profile's provider. Additive; no IPC schema change. Commit cb498088a. (Team Member)
- [260616_1527] [User-facing][Important] Library scan renderer-OOM / stuck-spinner crash (Bug 2) — on large (often cloud-synced) workspaces the file tree grew unbounded and exhausted renderer memory: the Library hung on "Scanning your files and folders…" indefinitely and at worst crash-looped the window (survived reinstall; downloading diagnostics also failed). The tree is now bounded by construction (100k-node / 128 MiB estimated file-tree budget, which indirectly bounds renderer memory), with honest partial-tree notices across every consumer (folders, cards, search, quick-open) instead of silent spin / fake-empty. A separate unguarded parse of oversized agent-event/tool-detail strings (including a dead truncation guard that always parsed the untruncated string) was hardened across ~12+ parse sites, and a cloud-listing failure that looked like an empty folder now fails loudly. No data loss — files on disk were intact. Commits 82c9e3f85, b7a801c29, d1479717c, a29ef1b39, df98c0e54, 008d964f6, d2c14ff39. (Team Member)
- [260616_1345] [User-facing][Important] Electron-42 embedding/GPU-worker crash + no-WebGPU device bug (REBEL-68M/68Q) — after the Electron 39→42 move (v0.4.47), the on-device embeddings gpu-worker crashed at startup via the WASM streaming-compilation path (~107 events / 65+ users, Electron-42-only); rerouted to onnxruntime's equivalent ArrayBuffer fallback to kill the crash by construction. Separately, on any machine without WebGPU the worker was handed an invalid `cpu` device (onnxruntime-web accepts only `webgpu`|`wasm`) and silently never initialised — embeddings still worked via the slower service-level node fallback, but the in-renderer worker didn't; now uses the correct `wasm` device, with a typed `selectEmbeddingDevice` making the invalid `cpu` value a compile error. A CI WASM boot-smoke gate (mac + Windows) was added to catch the class. Commits faa9a4b15, 3e641965f, a9d0b77a2, 6e1cda89e. (Team Member)
- [260616_1258] [User-facing][Important] Mid-stream transient retry no longer duplicates assistant output — a transient error after result text had begun streaming re-ran the turn from scratch and folded the partial into the result, persisting duplicated text (worst on unattended/automation turns; third recurrence of this family). Once any result text has streamed, a transient error now ends the turn cleanly with a retryable terminal instead of silently re-sending; pre-text clean retries are preserved. Applied to both the Anthropic and OpenAI client paths. Commit 6ce3afbab. (Team Member)
- [260616_1334] [User-facing][Important] One malformed session no longer collapses the whole conversation index — a single bad conversation file crashed the index rebuild, aborting it and leaving nearly all conversations invisible in the sidebar/folders (one case ~2,735 → 67); triggered by an index-version bump interacting with multiple builds against shared data. The rebuild now isolates/repairs the bad session rather than aborting, self-heals a suspiciously short index from on-disk files, recovers the full list even in a read-only state, and reports catastrophic index-load failures instead of silently emptying the sidebar. No data loss — files were intact. Commits bd8c1d199, 577d99168, cabaf6f1a. (Team Member)
- [260616_1658] [User-facing] Behind-the-scenes safety check stops failing closed on Opus 4.7/4.8 (REBEL-64Y) — the BTS wire sanitizer + safety assert were keyed on `thinkingAlwaysOn` (Fable-5-only), so Opus 4.7/4.8 — which also reject temperature/top_p/top_k with a 400 but aren't always-on-thinking — leaked those params through. Only the safety-eval's local self-heal was protected; watchdog-judge and operator-consult BTS paths weren't, so the safety eval failed closed and blocked the user's tool for the growing cohort whose BTS model resolved to Opus 4.8 (the default). Adds a distinct `samplingParamsForbidden` catalog axis (Fable 5 + Opus 4.7/4.8) stripped at the shared chokepoint, while the max_tokens floor / thinking-config rejection stay on `thinkingAlwaysOn`. Commit 64b3bec7c. (Team Member)
- [260615_1759] [User-facing] "Mark as done" restored for foldered conversations — the per-conversation "Mark as done" action had gone missing for conversations inside a folder. Commit 9ee6caf9e. (Team Member)
- [260615_1326] [User-facing] App shell no longer scrolls off-screen when adding a custom model — opening "Add a model" in Settings → Agents & Voice could push the whole app shell sideways out of view. Commit 4c573a2af. (Team Member)
- [260616_1247] [User-facing] Model selector shows the default tier after recovery — an effort-only post-recovery state showed an empty "Custom" label instead of the default tier with a thinking qualifier. Commit ca8ce4a3b. (Team Member)

### Developer-facing & Infrastructure
- [260616_1824] [Developer-facing] GPU-worker WASM-smoke now exercises the real crash path offline (REBEL-68M/68Q residual) — vendors a small local model (`Xenova/all-MiniLM-L6-v2`) under `private/test-fixtures/` and adds init-only `modelName`/`dtype` overrides to the gpu-worker (production omits them → default model + fp32) so headless CI can load offline and still hit the exact onnxruntime-web WASM-compile crash path — closing the smoke gate's "can't physically run in CI" gap from the original fix. Commit 74ef9826f. (Team Member)
- [260616_1658] [Developer-facing] Recovery-seam stale-fold hardening (observability only) — added a non-fatal observable invariant that logs (lengths only, never content) if a recovery-seam fold ever grows the persisted result via a stale partial — a defensive monitor layered on the mid-stream dedup fix, with no evidence of a real field occurrence; a follow-up reset stops it false-firing on a normal tool-using turn. No user-visible change. Commits 5b4a8149f, 2fbacb1ff. (Team Member)

## [0.4.47] — 2026-06-11 to 2026-06-15

### Added
- [260614_1822] [User-facing] Done conversations stay inside their folder on the Active tab — finished work inside a folder now appears in a collapsed-by-default "Done (N)" group beneath the folder's active conversations, so a folder stays self-contained instead of hiding finished work in the Done tab. Done rows are muted but fully functional; collapsed state persists per folder; navigating to a done conversation expands its folder and group one-shot. All-done folders still drop to the Done tab. Commit ac93d96b8. (Team Member)
- [260613_1628] [User-facing][Important] Desktop engine upgraded Electron 39 → 42 — moved from Electron 39.8.6 (EOL since 2026-05-05, no security patches) to 42.4.0 with newer Chromium and a current Node runtime. De-risked by a measurement spike (packaged build, boot, full E2E fleet, fsevents shutdown path; green on macOS arm64/Intel and Windows). Key finding: the fsevents-leak sweep/guards are permanent — on Electron ≥41 an unswept leak converts the old quit-time crash into an indefinite telemetry-blind quit deadlock (FOX-3487). Also fixed a Windows native-inventory checker case bug (`resources` path casing). No user action; the app auto-updates. Commits cb8acf380, 6bd5d90e8, 7c6c32ab9, 4875a274, e6cac783. (Team Member)
- [260612_2156] [User-facing][Open Source] Slack "send yourself a note" now actually notifies you — Slack treats a DM you send to yourself as already-read, so notes Rebel jotted into your self-DM never produced a notification. A new `send_myself_a_note` tool delivers the note as a DM from the Rebel bot (which Slack does notify on), needs only `chat:write` (no re-auth), lands in a separate thread from your own self-DM, and the old send-as-yourself path now routes through the notifying path. Published as slack@0.1.6; source public at github.com/mindstone/mcp-servers. Commits 4e16cc21, f402197d. (Team Member)
- [260612_2156] [User-facing][Open Source] Salesforce BYOK OAuth credentials now resolve from settings — Salesforce is BYOK (you supply your own Connected App key/secret): the setup UI saved them to settings, but the resolver read only env plus the empty injected provider, so typed credentials were orphaned and start-auth failed with "Salesforce OAuth credentials not configured". Resolution is now env → settings → provider for both start-auth consumers (IPC and bridge), and the status diagnostic uses the same resolver. Published as salesforce@0.1.3; source public at github.com/mindstone/mcp-servers. Commits 6d2f253f, 6b5d8160, a27dc8cf. (Team Member)
- [260612_1200] [User-facing][Important] Model enable/disable toggle — each model in Settings → Agents & Voice → Available models now shows a clear On/Off toggle in the action row, replacing a bare checkbox that was easy to miss. Toggle a model off to stop it appearing as a choice, without removing it from your list; toggle it back on when you want it again. (Team Member)
- [260612_1200] [User-facing][Important] Add-a-model dialog: search and plan-aware grouping — the "Add a model" dialog now has a live search box (filter by name or provider), a "Recommended for most people" shortlist, and — for users on a Mindstone plan — an "Included with your plan" group surfacing the models their subscription covers so they're one click away. (Team Member)
- [260612_1130] [User-facing] Settings → Usage revamped — rich power-user drilldown restored beneath a clean glance. A May-8 chief-designer cleanup (`7d0b8a72d`) had gutted the Usage tab from ~949 LOC to ~125, stripping (without user authorisation) the Last-24h view, the costliest-conversation/turn "Records", per-model / per-payment-method / per-automation breakdowns, the daily table, CSV export, monthly projection, trend, and cache-hit ratio — while keeping the (good) spend-quality waterfall. The backend data layer (`getUsageInsights`, `getDailyBreakdown`, `byModel`/`byAuthMethod`/`byAutomationType`) was fully intact, so this is a restore-and-merge: one page, three progressive-disclosure tiers on the existing `SettingSection advanced` accordion — Tier 0 glance (period incl. **Last 24h**, honest hero, waterfall verbatim, category bars with inline sub-category expand exposing previously-hidden background-compaction cost), Tier 1 four default-collapsed drilldowns (Where it went by model/payment/automation · The Records with click-through · Day by day with table + CSV + a UTC-day note · Efficiency stats), Tier 2 tooltips. Tier-1 fetches degrade independently with a visible "Couldn't load" badge (never silent-hide, never fail the page). CSS migrated fully to design tokens (light + dark). Commits b01513170, 95131e642. (Team Member)
- [260611_1900] [User-facing] Frontier quality tier—the conversation quality slider gains a fifth notch ("Frontier", $$$$$) mapping working + thinking to `claude-fable-5` at xhigh effort; the rebel-settings MCP `set_quality_tier` tool and bridge route accept the new tier with matching copy. Strictly explicit opt-in: tier names are never persisted (selections write resolved model ids), so no existing setting or conversation migrates to Fable, existing Opus 4.8 "Maximum" users keep their label (reverse-match pinned by tests), and behind-the-scenes model selection is structurally untouched. Maximum's copy and the multi-model third-party swap (scoped to `maximum`) are unchanged. (Team Member)
- [260611_1700] [User-facing][Important] Claude Fable 5—Anthropic's new top-tier model (`claude-fable-5`) is now selectable for every role (Planner, Main work, Behind the scenes) with a direct Anthropic key or via OpenRouter: 1M-token context, 128K output, always-on adaptive reasoning, premium pricing (~2× Opus 4.8). Defaults are unchanged — Opus 4.8 remains the default thinking model and no existing model was deprecated. Shipped with runtime hardening so the model's stricter wire contract can't break the app: behind-the-scenes calls automatically drop sampling parameters the model rejects (compile-time enforced, plus a runtime wire assertion and a CI transport-symmetry guard), safety-classifier refusals are recognised and surfaced honestly (no tool execution from a refused response, no futile auto-retry), and an unavailable Fable degrades gracefully to Opus 4.8. Commits 65e44e7ba, d37d3841b, bb504cf01, 3daf6e70c, e7ea8eb6c, adce393c9, 5b785e782. (Team Member)

### Fixed
- [260616_0530] [User-facing][Important] ChatGPT/Codex reconnect auth bug (FOX-3494) — a ChatGPT-Pro user was fully blocked for a week: Settings showed "connected" yet every turn failed "ChatGPT is not connected", and reconnecting didn't help. Diagnosis (4 diverse-model passes + decisive PostHog telemetry; REBEL-68Z) found two code paths that strand a Codex-only user on the non-credentialed Anthropic provider and fail closed with `connection-not-configured`. Two targeted fixes (robust to both, since the user's exact state wasn't retrievable): **(A)** new shared-core `applyCodexProviderHeal` heals `activeProvider → 'codex'` only when the current state is unusable (`codexConnected && activeProvider !== 'codex' && !hasUsableCredentialFor(activeProvider)`, treating `undefined`/`null` as unusable), fired cross-surface on `codex:login` success + cloud `handleCodexTokens` route + a post-bootstrap version-gated boot heal, with the automation catch-up sweep guard reading the post-heal provider and `provider_heal_applied` telemetry; **(B)** the `claude-*`-under-codex route-time divert now mints an actionable terminal (`missing-anthropic-credentials-for-claude-model`, primary-turn-scoped via `isPrimaryTurnRole`, both settings + profile arms gated on `activeProvider==='codex'`) carrying a `switch-model` recovery that collapses the conversation to a codex-servable GPT across all model-state layers (global + session overrides + per-turn) and both roles — with a capture-before-await stale-session guard — instead of a misleading "Anthropic needs a key" dead-end; BTS/subagent/background divert preserved (260501). Telemetry now stamps the true culprit (`routeInvalidReason`/`failedRouteRole`/`unsupportedModelId`) alongside the route-target provider, which had masked the root cause for a week. Findings (two-user pattern, route-time dead-end, provider-stamp masking) fed back to the parked `260611_provider_error_architecture` thread. Commits 1997aed6e, c1bfe289c, 6d8931077, 0cdf8899f, 4863454da, 61a762d06. (Team Member)
- [260612_2215] [User-facing] BillingBadge tooltips no longer mislabel the active provider. Commit 49f995a40. (Team Member)
- [260612_2030] [User-facing][Important] Context-state compaction no longer fails ~97% of the time — the behind-the-scenes `compaction-bts` call (`updateContextStateViaLLM`) emits the full cumulative JSON context-state but capped output at `maxTokens: 2000`, so any faithful state >2000 tokens truncated mid-JSON → `JSON.parse` failed → `ok:false` → prune skipped ("to prevent data loss") → still billed. Confirmed in one dev's cost ledger: 229/250 attempts `auxiliary_failed`, 241/250 with `outTok` pinned at exactly 2000, ~98% of `compaction-bts` spend wasted on failures; the skipped prune also fed context-exhaustion (FOX-2857 family). Fixes: (1) cap raised to `CONTEXT_STATE_UPDATE_MAX_TOKENS=8192` (~3.4× the largest of 2106 measured real states, max ~2331 tok); (2) `boundContextState()` caps each append-prone category to the most-recent 40 deduped items + bounds the rolling summary, so the cumulative state can't grow past the cap across prunes (the prompt instructs the model never to delete — unbounded-growth class killed by construction); (3) hardened extraction — collect all text blocks (was `content[0]` only) + a fence/prose-robust balanced-brace scanner replacing the greedy `/\{.*\}/s`; (4) in-function truncation detection (`stopReason`→`failureReason`) surfaced to the cost ledger as the new `auxiliary_failed reason:'truncated'` (added to the shared `FailureReason` vocabulary + its zod mirrors) instead of the catch-all `'other'`, plus a near-cap (>80%) warning; (5) internal timeout 30s→60s so the larger cap isn't aborted mid-generation. Verified with a live red→green repro on DeepSeek V4 Flash + Haiku (via OpenRouter) and 18 deterministic unit tests. Follow-up (spun out): routing compaction to the cheap BTS/background model — a now-marginal cost optimization (the dominant waste was failures, now fixed) carrying an auth/routing fork that needs its own focused change. See `docs/plans/260612_compaction-state-cap/PLAN.md`. (Team Member)
- [260612_1130] [User-facing][Important] Usage "Total spend" no longer overstates what you actually paid — the cost ledger records API-equivalent value for every turn, including subscription-covered ones, so the old hero presented (e.g.) ~$1,800 as if paid out-of-pocket when ~86% was covered by a ChatGPT/Mindstone subscription (real out-of-pocket ~$130). The hero now leads with an honest "You paid" (known out-of-pocket only), frames subscription coverage as good-news context, and shows pre-cost-tracking/unclassifiable spend on its own line — the four buckets reconcile to total value. Two attribution fixes underpin it: `mindstone-managed` is now correctly classified as subscription-covered (374 ledger rows were mis-counted as paid), and the `unknown`/unattributable bucket is no longer folded into "You paid". Background context-compaction cost is also now stamped with the parent turn's payment method (it previously fell into the out-of-pocket bucket). Commit b01513170. (Team Member)
- [260612_0250] [User-facing][Developer-facing] Calendar sync warnings hardened—sync warnings are now structured data (typed at the writer chokepoints) with account identifiers scrubbed before they are persisted or sent to telemetry, closing a path that could leak account emails (including `%40`-encoded forms) into diagnostics; the "Calendar sync has not run yet" warning no longer false-fires on fresh profiles (time-bounded gate instead of a bare has-synced flag); and CI now detects exports whose only consumers are tests (knip production-mode leg + diff-guard), catching the dead-recovery-path class where "covered" code is actually unreachable from the app. Commits 165972339, be565f5b8, 3f2f0cce9, 7a3946260, a7ab0af4e. (Team Member)
- [260611_2247] [User-facing] "Calendar Cache needs attention" launch nag killed — a Google Workspace account with an expired sign-in latched a persisted warning that re-toasted on every app launch (toast dedup is in-memory only), blamed the healthy calendar cache, and deep-linked to a connectors panel that couldn't show which account was broken. Four-part fix: (1) `calendarCacheHealth` joins the first-report toast suppression set (Help-menu glow + issue count still show pre-existing warns); (2) the persisted needs-reconnect latch structurally cannot outlive its account — cleared at the disconnect chokepoint and on reconnect, with a config-keyed orphan sweep each sync cycle that also heals already-stale entries; (3) Settings → Connectors now pinpoints the affected Google Workspace account ("Sign-in expired" row + a Reconnect action that re-auths exactly that email, mismatched-account callbacks rejected), and the health deep-link auto-selects it; (4) reconnect conditions now have ONE channel — reauth warnings no longer enter the persisted calendar cache (skipped-account counts stay in sync telemetry), so the surviving toast is the provider-truthful "Google Workspace needs reconnecting" and the double toast for a single expired sign-in is gone. Commits 0548e10ec, e243b4858, 8080881c0, a65dbab04, 759104356, 7c2d78766. (Team Member)
- [260611_1825] [User-facing][Developer-facing] REBEL-5D5 renderer memory retention — conversation panes now remount per session, so TanStack Virtual's message-keyed `elementsCache` cannot keep detached DOM/fiber trees from earlier conversations reachable across session switches. The external height cache remains intact for scroll restoration; within-one-session cache eviction is tracked separately. (Team Member)
- [260611_1810] [User-facing][Important] File search no longer exhausts file descriptors—the file-search Node fallback leaked one open file descriptor per scanned file (a large workspace accumulated ~19k), eventually pushing fd numbers past the OS limit so every subsequent subprocess spawn failed with `EBADF` (Bash, file search, and other helpers all dead until app restart). The read stream is now deterministically destroyed per file, scanning stops once the match-overflow cap is crossed (instead of opening every remaining file), and binary detection reads a bounded 512 bytes via open/read/close instead of whole files. Commit 6adf55525. (Team Member)
- [260611_1745] [User-facing][Important] In-app bug reports reach Sentry again—reports from Beta builds had been silently discarded since 06-10 (~8 lost, while the app logged "ingested" and users saw "sent"): string truncation (including the Sentry SDK's own post-hook truncation) could split a surrogate pair (e.g. an emoji), leaving an unpaired UTF-16 surrogate that Sentry's processing pipeline rejects as `invalid_json`, dropping the whole envelope including attachments — after returning HTTP 200. Outgoing events are now swept to well-formed UTF-16 at the shared `redactSentryEvent` chokepoint (all surfaces; error + transaction hooks), in-repo truncation is surrogate-safe (`truncateWellFormed`), and the transport log + confirmation toast now claim only what is verified (2xx = accepted by transport, not delivered). Commits 71e80c621, 42b4a7c8e. (Team Member)
- [260611_1518] [User-facing] Relaunch onboarding offers the intro again—after Settings → "Relaunch onboarding", re-completing the setup wizard could land on a Home with no "Start here" activation card and therefore no path to the onboarding coach: the relaunch reset's hand-rolled field list had drifted from the activation-card suppression signals, leaving a stale `onboardingChecklist.completedSteps[0]`. Both now share one SSOT helper (`hasCoachCompletionSignal`/`clearCoachCompletionState`) so the lists can't drift again, guarded by drift-killer unit tests and a new seeded E2E asserting the post-onboarding Home activation card (the assertion gap that let this ship). Relaunch deliberately does NOT reset tutorial-checklist progress. Commits 01e941774, f5888fbe8. (Team Member)
- [260611_1010] [User-facing][Developer-facing] Idle CPU churn — killed five stateless re-derivation loops that kept the main process busy at idle, seeded by a live diagnosis of the installed beta (~6k log lines/hr + 189%/375% multi-core idle bursts). (1) **Cloud-pull convergence**: a never-converging pull loop (33 files re-downloading then failing `mkdir` every ~5-min cycle, 1,749 fail pairs/22h, root cause: two dangling Drive symlinks) now has a per-file failure memo + backoff + terminal-vs-transient classification + pre-download preflight, so any persistent per-file failure is harmless (≤1 warn + bounded backoff). (2) **Oversized-push memo** (keyed on manifest hash): 7–50MB files stop re-entering the push set and forcing a second full workspace walk every cycle. (3) **`checkStaleEmbeddings` count gate**: a summary-level `userMessageCount` delta gate stops the full 622MB / ~2,800-file corpus parse every 5 focused minutes. (4) **`time-saved-repair` summary prefilter** (cutoff−7d margin) + scan-once: launch-time corpus parses drop from up to 13 to ≤1. (5) **`file_neighbors` checkpoint**: a `(chunksMutationVersion, fileNeighborsEpoch)` converged checkpoint + deterministic-failure memo + trigger coalescing make idle no-op fill passes O(1) (~105 full scans/hr → ~0 at idle). The "Preserving legacy … status entries" warn flood (~2,295/pass) was demoted to debug + per-process deduped + replaced by a single first-detection summary line. See `docs/plans/260611_perf-idle-churn/PLAN.md`. Commits 414f8fa09..7c96eba57. (Team Member)

- [260614_1359] [Developer-facing] TS error-ratchet stale-deps guard — the ratchet now fails loud on unresolved-module (TS2307) errors instead of silently miscounting (a missing sub-project dep suppresses downstream diagnostics → local-green/CI-red); the mobile TS baseline was floored 2→0 via `@types/async-lock`. Commits b900f56c, bb47ccaa. (Team Member)
- [260614_1039] [Developer-facing][Important] Cloud-sync session-events outbox idempotency fix (REBEL-68C) — the idempotency key fingerprinted event identities, not the full append body, so a retry with a drifted `metadataPatch`/`baseSeq`/message-body produced the same key with a different body → server HTTP 500. The key now covers the exact server field set / full body. Commit b35f7380. (Team Member)
- [260614_0937] [Developer-facing] Process docs — added NEW_PROVIDER_SUPPORT_PROCESS and SMART_MODEL_PICKING docs, renamed PUSH_TO_BETA/PUSH_TO_PRODUCTION → RELEASE_TO_*, and led the weekly review with a demand-driven hot-list (retiring broad index-mining fan-outs). Commits 9af88a0d, 017bd550, 9c78d6de, f11690b9. (Team Member)
- [260614_0135] [Developer-facing] Recs-drain rounds 7–8: by-construction CI guards — a batch of static guards from the recommendations drain: markdown-url-guard sibling-parity, MCP catalog local-file-sandbox metadata plus bridge-state check, postmortem augment-line integrity, Forge heap-prefix and universal strict-tsconfig-flag gates, safety/tool-scope/path-containment guards, a typecheck-coverage ratchet for validate:fast-wired scripts, an E2E startup safety-timeout vs perf-budget gate, exhaustive `assertNever` over install-completion, branded live-meeting id types, opaque lease-owner identity, operator-field-precedence and botqa-privacy gates, and an observable internal-changelog archive. Commits 8f500b33, fb6891c4, ec20c598, 8e8747e4, a2580c8c, fbd97a88, 7fa1218f, 383082d7b, 2b06946a, 499622ac, 35be2855. (Team Member)
- [260613_1830] [Developer-facing][Important] Sub-agent `max_tokens` clamp now uses the concrete routed backend — council/ad-hoc dispatch clamped `max_tokens` against the alias route-table model ("working") instead of the concrete routed backend, so e.g. Haiku-under-GPT got a 128k>64k 400. It now clamps against the concrete routed backend; reasoning-replay is keyed the same way. Commits b8ae88c0, 5906daca. (Team Member)
- [260613_0034] [Developer-facing][Important] Mobile identified error monitoring and client analytics — the React Native app gained identified Sentry error monitoring plus health context, an iOS privacy manifest and production Sentry symbol upload, and always-on identified RudderStack client-side analytics emitting only client/UI events disjoint from core (no double-count). Commits c2575d06, 6c74a996, 271a2c24, c62c4393, a49910c4, 7cb5152b, 0da2d0ad. (Team Member)
- [260613_0000] [Developer-facing] Silent-swallow ESLint gate is now diff-scoped — retired the churning count-baseline ratchet for a diff-scoped new-warnings gate (fail-closed on non-infra errors), kept `--max-warnings 3000` as backstop, and added a rule-presence smoke test. A shared `resolveBaseSha` merge-base fallback that leaked across consumers was made opt-in after a full-gate catch. Commits 01d8eef7, 317384100, 0a96bd4d, 7554ade3, 50fde9be, 4214db75. (Team Member)
- [260612_2210] [Developer-facing] CI desktop unit-test reliability — the desktop unit-test job is now matrix-sharded across three runners, two slow desktop tests had real poll/dispose waits collapsed, the test-gate scope is documented, plus a flake postmortem. Commits ad42ac08, 91856b94, 03d19ed1, a510a9f6, 32027ac2. (Team Member)
- [260612_2037] [Developer-facing] Compaction failure attribution (Stage B) — follow-on to the compaction-cap fix at 260612_2030: truncated compaction failures are now attributed honestly in the cost ledger, and the JSON extractor stays balance-based with parse-error logging. Commits bcf4b9a2, e783e3c3, e7457284. (Team Member)
- [260611_1010] [Developer-facing] Peak-burst attribution — the periodic `Memory diagnostic` emission now carries `peakAtMs` + `peakTopProcesses` (top ≤3 processes `{label, pid, cpuPercent}` at the peak-sample instant) alongside `totalCpuPercentPeak`, so a post-ship idle-CPU burst check can name the process at the peak instant instead of inferring it. Per-peak-sample, not continuous profiling. Commit 414f8fa09. (Team Member)

## [0.4.46] — 2026-06-02 to 2026-06-11

> Spans the **0.4.45 production release** (2026-06-04). The internal changelog never carried a separate 0.4.45 section, so the changes that shipped as 0.4.45 are documented here alongside the post-release 0.4.46 work. The user-facing equivalents are split across the `v0.4.45` and `v0.4.46` sections of `rebel-system/help-for-humans/changelog.md`.

### Added
- [260611_1139] [User-facing] Onboarding & transfer copy polish—the first-run primary CTA is now **"Start now"** (was "Start fresh"), the "Start fresh instead" abandon-state copy is unified across the import flows, the transfer affordance is demoted with clearer fresh-start framing, and the "Finish settling in" settings notice is gated to transfers and moved to the bottom of the Workspace tab. Commits e7d917645, 080b2cf15, 666f85148, 77e5bff8f, 00269f12d. (Team Member)
- [260611_1032] [User-facing][Developer-facing] "Tools are back online" toast—when Rebel's MCP tool router (super-mcp) recovers after a surfaced failure, you now get a one-shot confirmation toast instead of silence. Under the hood, `use_tool` gained a Zod dispatch parse that returns a coded `-33003` for the whole missing-required-field class, with a staged short-circuit that runs before dispatch validation. Commit 20ced7fe5; super-mcp 92f0c0c, f244a40. (Team Member, Team Member)
- [260610_0031] [User-facing] Automations Desktop/Cloud—the ambiguous chameleon cloud badge is replaced by an explicit **Desktop | Cloud** segmented control, and connector cards now show a clear **"queued"** state (instead of a silently-spinning button) when a connect/disconnect/setup-save/per-account-disconnect is deferred behind an in-progress task. The deferred-event matcher was tightened to exact-context so a simultaneous unrelated connector op can't light up the wrong card. Commits c3e6c7f9c, 4b49787d5, 40c62848, e7a00c1b. (Team Member, Team Member)
- [260609_2357] [User-facing][Important] Migrate Rebel between machines—a new one-time migration feature: export your Rebel setup (settings + data) to a `.rebeltransfer` bundle from Settings → Workspace ("Move to a new computer"), then import it during onboarding on the new machine, finishing with a guided "re-auth checklist". Exports are read-only on the source and strip secrets/credentials by construction (classification SSOT, CI-gated); imports validate the untrusted bundle (zip-slip/size-bomb/tampered-content guards), stage into a sibling dir, and only publish onto a fresh profile—always moving any existing data aside to a recoverable backup. Privacy-safe transfer diagnostics included. Shipped to dev; UI live-verified (export + checklist) with the onboarding-import branch covered by unit tests. Commits 3bcf01e6c, 697f49005, 090f31479, f01f17b36, 8c9c3df12, 799c3e782 (+12 more). (Team Member)
- [260609_1704] [User-facing][Open Source] New Xero connector—a Rebel-owned `@mindstone/mcp-server-xero` MCP package lets the agent work with Xero (invoices incl. attachments/history/notes and **multi-currency invoice support**, plus contacts, payments, bank transactions and more), published as 0.0.17 with portal-visible custom-connection OAuth scopes so setup completes correctly and a currency-write guard. Source is public at github.com/mindstone/mcp-servers. Commits (mcp-servers) ad9c528, df0ac54, 0747dad; (main) fa13ae12, 742f7742, a913a9e96. (Team Member)
- [260609_1156] [User-facing] Decision-first approval cards—approval dialogs now lead with the decision (durable "allow" choices stay primary), make the preview an opt-in confidence affordance rather than the focus, and explain safety pauses in plainer language; inbox approval cards regained title-based preview routing, and the conversation/markdown column got calmer, less boxed-in styling. Commits a0a771ca9, a134d617f, 4564a0969, 59a1ed7bc, 2bf4ddc80. (Team Member)
- [260608_2350] [User-facing][Open Source] Clear connector setup guidance—connecting an integration that isn't configured (the default in OSS/self-built builds, where you supply your own OAuth credentials) now opens a structured `ConnectorSetupDialog` with provider-accurate, step-by-step setup instructions instead of a generic "not configured" toast. Guidance flows end-to-end through the shared start-auth IPC schema so every connect surface (connections panel, onboarding, Slack messaging, DigitalOcean) shows the same help, backed by a class-kill guard. Commits 85e6a1c1, 7a68e75b, 310ea325, 055f1664, 9d316368. (Team Member)
- [260608_2051] [User-facing][Open Source] Editable space organisation name—you can now rename a space's organisation at any time by clicking its badge (which opens the Edit Space wizard with a "Space updated" toast), not just during onboarding; this also closed the last real gap in OSS self-config (which replaced server-side `/api/config` provisioning). Commit a0bc83b0; README rewritten for the public OSS launch (51a0aa32). (Team Member)
- [260608_0305] [User-facing][Open Source] OSS telemetry is opt-in—open-source builds never send analytics or crash data unless you explicitly enable it in Developer settings and supply your own keys (no fallback DSN). Added the opt-in toggle + progressive-disclosure credential inputs in the Developer tab, OSS-only. Commits ad4ea218, 16cf3309, ff755b46, 8864f90c. (Team Member)
- [260607_0756] [User-facing][Open Source] Bring-your-own-key meeting recorder—with your own Recall API key you can record and transcribe meetings directly (via the desktop SDK) instead of routing through Mindstone's meeting-bot worker, and in-progress transcripts are no longer lost across app restarts or key changes (a persisted transport/uploadId discriminator + safe-resume closes a silent-transcript-loss class). The enterprise/blank-key path is byte-for-byte unchanged. Commit e7e0331d1. (Team Member)
- [260606_1029] [User-facing] Composer Alt+Enter—while the agent is busy, Alt/Option+Enter now **queues** your message (same as plain Enter) instead of forcing a send-now + interrupt; send-now is now reachable only via the explicit "Send now" button. This removes an accidental-supersede footgun; the tips strip, Shortcuts dialog, bundled help, and four UI docs were synced (and a pre-existing "Interrupt" mislabel corrected). Commit b152c25b7; rebel-system bfd8def. (Team Member)
- [260605_1914] [User-facing][Important] External userData backup—a new background service takes copy-only, **external** (sibling-of-userData, so it survives a userData reset) timestamped snapshots of a curated allowlist: settings, OAuth/API tokens, connector credentials, contributions, automations, memory, inbox, focus/tasks, safety-trust, plugin state, and the cost-ledger. Snapshots use a locked-down secret vault (0700/0600 perms), sha256-and-size-only manifests (never the secret values), a 24h launch throttle, and manifest-gated retention (newest 10 + 30-day prune + 200MB total-size budget, always keeping ≥1, symlink/type-guarded). It runs fire-and-forget at startup, never throws into boot, and never mutates the originals. A Stage-2 secret-hygiene pass writes settings and `super-mcp-router.json` at 0600 and scrubs secrets from migration/pre-cloud backup copies via a shared `SENSITIVE_KEY_PATTERN` SSOT; at-rest `safeStorage` encryption is deferred. Commits c7e8fb0ae, d8d2c2a34, e426f8568. (Team Member)
- [260603_0800] [User-facing] New model—MiniMax M3 (`minimax/minimax-m3`) is now selectable for OpenRouter users: a 512K-context frontier model with reasoning and tool support, registered as both a main and auxiliary (behind-the-scenes) model. A new `ADDING_AN_OPENROUTER_MODEL` runbook documents the onboarding path so future additions derive every downstream registry (model map, presets, dropdowns) from a single catalog entry. Commits e42c7b102, 2592b71ae, f40090d76. (Team Member)
- [260602_1541] [User-facing][Developer-facing][Important] bulk_export tool restored—the native `bulk_export` meta-tool (which lets the agent export your data in bulk) was re-landed in super-mcp and re-registered at the MCP seam after a super-mcp submodule-pin rollback had silently orphaned it. The re-land adds context-safety, partial-status reporting, path hardening, cancellation, and atomic no-clobber writes (no empty file left on failure), plus a kill-by-construction guard and a live skip-green spike so the regression class can't recur. The rebel-system skill doc was reconciled with the revived native tool. Commits b408c6bb2, e369bcd0f, 7aac52163, 3e432977e, ef6ef174e; super-mcp 2825951, 4ff7ed6, fc7fd6f; rebel-system df68985. (Team Member)

### Fixed
- [260611_1340] [User-facing] Honest rate-limit errors—when a ChatGPT Pro (or other non-Claude) model hit a rate limit mid-task and recovery couldn't switch models, Rebel showed the generic "Something went wrong mid-conversation… try sending your message again" — anti-advice for a rate limit. That terminal path now surfaces provider-aware rate-limit copy (the words "rate limit" included), and `Automation Run Failed` telemetry additionally records `errorKind` + a redacted, bounded `rawError` so support can distinguish rate limits from auth failures in PostHog without Sentry spelunking. Routing/retry/cooldown behaviour deliberately unchanged. Commits 5816a6418, c5c3ca17d, 36ff828ae. (Team Member)
- [260611_1106] [User-facing][Important] Sidebar folders survive cloud migration—conversation folders (the sidebar groupings you create to organise chats) were silently dropped when you migrated to the cloud or restored onto a new machine, because the `sessions/folders.json` sidecar (folder definitions + session→folder membership) was uploaded nowhere and pulled nowhere. The cloud round-trip now carries folders through upload and restore (with a renderer refresh, a boundary guard, and prune), killing the data-loss class by construction via a round-trip contract test. Commits 97d20cc3f, bb27d5507, 2c7cfb680, 1e32811be, 527fcfa94, 662f8c49e. (Team Member)
- [260611_1134] [User-facing] No more stuck reveal mask—a pending history-scroll "reveal" mask could get stuck on screen after switching sessions; it now self-cancels when both its origin and target sessions are gone (mark-time orphan guard), and a superseding mark clears any stale deferred target (FOX-3040 preservation intact). Commits 5386722d4, f9df4a54c. (Team Member)
- [260611_1034] [User-facing] Honest app-close interruption signal—a turn cut off because the app closed or restarted used to render a WifiOff icon + "Rebel was interrupted", which users misread as lost connectivity. It's now source-aware: shutdown shows a Power icon + "Rebel was closed", a startup correction shows "Rebel restarted", and the WifiOff / "Connection dropped" presentation is reserved for genuine transient-network drops (FOX-2771). Commit df63deb6b. (Team Member)
- [260611_0946] [User-facing][Open Source] Slack connects with saved tokens—the Slack connector now serves saved tokens without requiring OAuth client credentials (refresh-only; `SLACK_CLIENT_ID`/`SLACK_CLIENT_SECRET` marked not-required), failing loud only when a rotating refresh genuinely needs absent creds. Published as slack@0.1.4; source public at github.com/mindstone/mcp-servers. Commits (mcp-servers) 432fa4a, d4abde9, f63875e, c13b30a, 8c9e26a, 150c9bf. (Team Member)
- [260611_1016] [User-facing] Consistent Settings labels—swept the remaining "Settings > Diagnostics" references to the visible "Settings → Advanced" label. Commit f6afe9793. (Team Member)
- [260611_1233] [Developer-facing] Key-capture scripts merge by default—the env key-capture scripts now merge into existing env files by default (hand-maintained lines survive a refresh), built on a shared env-capture core; the legacy-eval-tokens allowlist follows the app-settings chokepoint to env-capture-core, and the privacy-canary test was split by sanitizer coverage to kill a raw-path flake. Commits 286467fe9, c197d5245, 9e83ff293, 578baaeb6, 7c03b551d, 101e2fdfc. (Team Member)
- [260610_0004] [User-facing][Important] Honest cloud teardown—when you tear down a cloud instance, the recovery banner now stays up (instead of falsely claiming success) if the remote instance may still be billing, partial-deprovision warnings render on the post-wipe local-mode screen you actually land on, and a `cloudTeardownGeneration` counter serializes managed reattach against destroy so a concurrent reattach can no longer silently revive a just-destroyed instance with stale credentials (C-F1/C-F2/C-F3). Commits 4dbcdfe2, a0d0fc26, ea830aec. (Team Member)
- [260609_2344] [User-facing][Important] Compose-card send no longer hangs silently—sending an email from a compose card could leave the Send button permanently disabled with no email sent and no error, when the host↔iframe reply was lost mid-handshake (FOX-3484/REBEL-677). The host now surfaces lost replies, and the google-workspace compose card bounds the wait with a ~75s timeout that re-enables the form with an honest "not sure if this sent—check your Sent folder" state (deliberately no auto-retry, since sending isn't idempotent). Commits (main) e154b2162, 5e3e8586d; (mcp-servers) ead058d. (Team Member)
- [260609_2339] [User-facing] No surprise macOS developer-tools dialog—the agent's Bash tool (and the Python setup/check skill) no longer trigger the OS "install Command Line Tools / download python3" popup on Macs without CLT installed; Python is now detected safely and the guard blocks the xcode-select shim exec path (FOX-3482/REBEL-674). Commits 61887de10, 4c86c4db5; rebel-system e1215d9f. (Team Member)
- [260609_2152] [User-facing] Memory updates on non-Anthropic providers—Codex/ChatGPT and other non-Anthropic users no longer hit a spurious "Anthropic API key" error when Rebel updates its memory; memory-update turns were inheriting a Claude thinking model that dragged in a plan-leg demanding an Anthropic key, now forced single-model by construction (FOX-3481). Commits d9b19646e, 63cbce84b, 201b1cd94, 3ffec8614. (Team Member)
- [260609_1521] [User-facing] Lower idle CPU/battery—Rebel clears a stuck `recording_local` status after a local recording stops and pauses CSS animations when the window is unfocused (not just hidden), cutting idle/background CPU and GPU usage (FOX-3438). Commits 9b311d194, 3711c08c6. (Team Member)
- [260609_1419] [User-facing] Connector & UI fixes—"Approve always" now persists for Microsoft 365 draft tools (FOX-3476), search clearly distinguishes "backend unavailable" from "no matches" (FOX-3003), and you get a toast if "Open in Finder"/file reveal fails instead of silent nothing (FOX-3422). Commits de9e29554, 56b068cd8, e371f19fe, 77ab309de. (Team Member)
- [260609_1406] [User-facing] Conversations recover from stalls—the core turn loop gained a dead-stream idle deadline (armed only after the first chunk) and per-tool-call fault isolation, so a hung model stream or a single failing tool call no longer stalls the whole turn. Commits 8ec337fe3, 4d666d422. (Team Member)
- [260609_0743] [User-facing] Correct model labels + safer MCP writes—model-role tooltips stop mislabeling on proxy/managed paths (the effective routed model is now recorded in the turn registry, FOX-3436), and an MCP write that needs confirmation is staged for approval instead of being silently hard-denied on the `ask_remote` TOCTOU (FOX-3477). Commits 9d164b63b, 3d55b22d5, 4b4748aa3. (Team Member)
- [260608_1953] [User-facing] Two Sentry-routed fixes—the Use-Case/Workflow Refresh automation was 400'ing on every run because Anthropic rejects `maxItems` on array fields (removed; count still enforced via prompt, FOX-3478), and the Bash builtin tool threw `spawn EBADF` in packaged/headless setups from a bad inherited stdin (now ignores stdin, FOX-3467). Commits 93232b45, fe1d39db. (Team Member)
- [260608_1245] [User-facing][Important] OAuth connectors restored for the commercial app—an OSS-scrub regression had silently stripped the embedded-credentials table and forced env-only OAuth, breaking all seven OAuth connectors (Slack, Google, HubSpot, GitHub, Microsoft, Plaud, DigitalOcean) for commercial users with no gate catching it. Restored via a credentials provider injected behind the `@private/mindstone` alias (env wins, then injected fallback; OSS stub returns null), with an always-on construction guard. Secret rotation before mirror-publish is a tracked follow-up. Commits 6c506108, 4378c7c6, 8ba66770. (Team Member)
- [260608_1038] [User-facing] Truthful "not connected" errors—a provider that was never connected/configured (Codex/ChatGPT Pro, OpenRouter, a missing Anthropic key, a missing managed key) is no longer misclassified as an auth failure with a false "your AI provider rejected the credentials" toast; it now says "connect it in Settings" with provider-aware copy, killed by construction via an exhaustive map over the typed provider-credential-state union. Commits 17dde9de, c77137ad, 9a57aea7. (Team Member)
- [260607_2137] [User-facing] Fewer Drive conflict copies—fixed a Google Drive cloud-sync conflict-copy recurrence where a missing intermediate directory made the sibling-suppression gate fail open (REBEL-62A), and added a matching server-side conflict-copy filter in the cloud manifest. The cloud silent auto-update + rollback is now observable, notifying you when the cloud service auto-recovers. Commits 3e7b734, dc28626, bac85ff. (Team Member)
- [260607_2047] [User-facing][Important] Batch of reported bug fixes—selecting GPT-5.5 (or other non-Anthropic models) for deep thinking no longer reverts (REBEL-5JN); the compose form no longer shows up permanently blank (the host now re-delivers the prefill on the iframe's `ready` signal, REBEL-5YD/5YE/609); document search scrolls to the first match with proper nav-arrow states (REBEL-5WF); email review cards render HTML formatting through a tightened sanitizer (REBEL-66G); and 403s are correctly classified as out-of-credits vs spend-cap vs auth (REBEL-66J/65G/5YW). Commits 13d1497, 86c26cd, e771ef5, c142c01, 788afa4. (Team Member)
- [260607_1850] [User-facing] Mobile stability—a `deferNativeCleanup` chokepoint plus a lint rule kills a class of TurboModule cleanup crash on teardown by construction, and diagnostic logs (fileLogSink + event buffer) are purged on logout. Commits a162ab1, c3dcfc. (Team Member)
- [260607_1813] [User-facing][Important] Stronger secret redaction—three drifted "sensitive key name" predicates were consolidated into one `isSensitiveKeyName()` SSOT, closing a live gap where `accessToken`/`idToken`/`writeKey`/`jwt` could survive the cloud→mobile settings-response/backup scrub; separately, Sentry log breadcrumbs are now scrubbed deny-by-default across desktop, cloud, and mobile, enforced by a static guard so a new breadcrumb source can't leak by omission. Commits f9c65f398, 3a70ca2, dcb80dd, 38b0ce1. (Team Member)
- [260607_0632] [User-facing][Important] No cross-account data leak on mobile—logging out or unpairing on mobile now fully wipes the previous account's local data (including FileSystem meeting recordings and native stores) via a single `wipeAllAccountScopedState()` manifest chokepoint, backed by a CI gate requiring every persistence-touching module to be covered. Commit d6801006. (Team Member)
- [260607_0600] [User-facing][Important] Cloud-sync failures detected reliably—the sync/drain feeders called `recordSuccess()` whenever an operation merely *resolved* even if internal items failed, so the failure cooldown never engaged and real outages were masked; a `CloudSyncOutcome` verdict type + single `recordCooldownVerdict()` chokepoint now compute a real verdict across all five feeders. Commit d64f45ebd. (Team Member)
- [260606_1843] [User-facing][Developer-facing][Important] Model-role health now matches reality—the Settings model UI derives each role's health from the **same** precedence core as the runtime resolver (`resolveModelRolePrecedence`), so the role rows, Smart-Picking toolbar, Model Team section, conversation-override panel, and quality-tier matching can no longer disagree with what the agent will actually run. Two long-standing contradictions are killed by construction: a deleted role profile no longer falsely promises "Using default model for now" (the runtime would throw), and a disabled-but-model-stringed profile is no longer flagged "needs setup" when the runtime runs it fine (now an informational "Using <model> for now / Review profile"). The recovery (long-context fallback) role gained its own scoped inline warning + "Pick fallback" CTA when its profile goes stale. Commits 50b9727a9, 293173fdc, 222e010ad, 70b0a298b, 81ad597bc, 3617005e3. (Team Member)
- [260606_1819] [User-facing][Important] Mobile recordings stuck in the offline queue now upload—voice/meeting recordings deferred on a busy session could sit in the offline upload queue indefinitely because the queue was passive (it only re-checked on foreground/reconnect/manual retry). The queue now self-rearms a single retry-drain timer keyed to the earliest pending item (online-only, scope-preserving, with an escalating 10s→30s→60s backoff that never counts against the retry/permanent-failure taxonomy), and Home/Conversations pull-to-refresh now drains the upload queue so "refresh" actually recovers stuck items. REBEL-663/5RG/5G6. Commits d7b6dc3c6, f1b7139f2, eab6464d6, 3cde632c9. (Team Member)
- [260606_1710] [User-facing][Important] Cloud-sync folder conflict copies—Rebel now also stops Google Drive/Dropbox **folder-level** conflict copies (e.g. `Project (1)/notes.md`) from propagating across machines, closing the gap left by the earlier file-only fix (REBEL-62A). Suppression is narrowed to unambiguously machine-minted folder shapes (Drive numbered-copy, Dropbox conflicted-copy) and sibling-gated so intentional `Copy of …` folders still sync, and all suppression now routes through a single `WorkspaceSyncPolicy` chokepoint so a future call-site can't silently drop the guard. Honest scope: this is containment, not a cure—it doesn't stop the provider from minting the first copy (that needs cross-machine single-writer authority, deferred). Closes REBEL-5QS. Commits 7a20e83d4, 8da7c6ee5, d78274ad3, 9c5552219, 4422e8c64. (Team Member)
- [260606_1640] [User-facing][Important] Mobile reliability—push-notification registration is now fully guarded so a native permission/registration failure (simulators, restricted devices, transient module errors) degrades gracefully instead of escaping as an unhandled rejection that retried on every effect re-run (REBEL-1CN; 255 Sentry events). `GestureHandlerRootView` is hoisted to wrap all three layout branches (loading, unpaired, paired) so gesture components no longer throw "must be a descendant of GestureHandlerRootView" on pre-pair screens (REBEL-170); a screen-mount smoke harness backstops the class. Commits 3bc13d5d9, e8a257c8c. (Team Member)
- [260606_1339] [User-facing][Developer-facing][Important] Direct-Anthropic dialect routing—fixed a routing rejection where a self-prefixed model id like `anthropic/claude-haiku-4-5` was fail-closed as a foreign proxy dialect on the direct-Anthropic path (it now strips the matching `anthropic/` self-prefix to a bare native id, while genuinely foreign ids—`openai/…`, `anthropic/not-claude`—still fail closed). - [260611_1408] [Developer-facing][Important] Faster, less-contended pushes to dev—two pre-push-gate levers shipped: (1) the `validate:fast` runner now resolves `npm run` steps to direct `node --import tsx` spawns at runtime (115/124 steps; package.json stays SSOT; a committed step-registry baseline + set-equality test makes silently dropping a guard a test failure by construction), cutting the gate 165→134s on the measuring machine; (2) `git-safe-sync` gained a same-host advisory sync lock (PID-liveness staleness, fail-open, `--no-lock` escape hatch, `lock-wait` telemetry span) so concurrent local agents queue instead of losing the push race after full validation — in June, 22% of 208 syncs (≥18 same-host) lost that race, burning ~12h. Cross-machine races remain; guard batching is a telemetry-gated follow-up. Same-day follow-ups: git-safe-sync now auto-aligns provably-safe submodule pointer-lag (kills the post-manual-merge "uncommitted changes" abort; never touches a submodule with local changes/commits) and auto-retries once on a structurally classified lost push race (non-FF rejection shape + verified remote movement; `[remote rejected]` never retries; `--no-retry` opt-out) — retried races stay visible to telemetry via `push-retry` notes. - [260606_1354] [Developer-facing][Important] Contract-coverage gates—the boundary-seam → contract-test coverage gate (I-2) was promoted from warn to enforce, a conflict-matcher consumer-set-completeness guard kills the detection≠prevention class, and new behavioural contracts (agent:turn + tool-safety:staged-execute IPC, real-verdict routing-depth, managed-OR ZDR/proxy-precedence, bundled-MCP spawn behind a built-artifact chokepoint) were wired in behind it. Commits 4297febf0, e90792e0d, 7b2af0ed8, 7b2a7bd29, dca34991f, db165f1a0, 16938d863, 6df2c534c, 10d6474bd. (Team Member)
- [260606_1331] [Developer-facing] super-mcp: `use_tool` now rejects a missing/empty `tool_id` with a coded, recoverable `ARG_VALIDATION_FAILED` error (with an actionable "use search_tools/list_tools" message) instead of a raw TypeError surfacing as a generic INTERNAL_ERROR. REBEL-62D. (Team Member)
- [260606_1211] [User-facing] OpenRouter attribution—managed/proxy OpenRouter requests now send the canonical app attribution (`rebel.mindstone.com` / "Rebel") on both egress paths instead of an unowned `mindstone.app` domain, sharing a single SSOT constant so the two paths can't drift again. Commit 2a62e7c2f. (Team Member)
- [260606_1155] [Developer-facing] Bug-report & Sentry diagnostics—the bug-report log filter was stringifying pino's nested `err` into `"[object Object]"` (e.g. 41× "Codex passthrough failed") and blanking the deterministic fallback's "Top Error Patterns"; a key-aware sanitizer now preserves canonical Error keys (dropping content-bearing custom props) and the rebel-system bug-report-analysis prompt was rewritten to be evidence-first (observed codes/counts/IDs, explicit hypotheses, a mandatory "Cannot Determine" section). Separately, the ci-e2e Sentry noise filter now matches `AgentSessionError` by exception *type* (the message never matched → REBEL-184/183/185 leaked into triage). Commits 947d790d4, d20fd6eed, c4c73f614; rebel-system 7c0c67b. (Team Member)
- [260606_1124] [Developer-facing] Local cloud-sync test harness—a real (non-mocked) fixture that spawns the actual cloud-service plus two real sync instances, a `DriveSim` conflict generator (file/folder/concurrent-edit), live integration tests, and an operator CLI; this is what reproduced and locked the REBEL-5QS folder leak. Commits 70fcf3de2, 9f9d1624f, b172bb9e1, 1263ef732, 16099279e. (Team Member)
- [260605_2236] [Developer-facing][Open Source] rebel-system OSS/catalog hygiene—dropped the internal-only investor-relations skill from the OSS-bundled rebel-system per the OSS dev-landable split, and corrected the `extend-mcp-server` rebel-oss fallback allowlist so it regained catalog↔skill set-equality (a transient mismatch had been blocking all pushes on origin/dev). rebel-system 5076bc0, 05eb9c8. (Team Member, Team Member)
- [260605_2002] [Developer-facing][Important] Knowledge-work eval correctness—a provider-agnostic canonical pricing module (OpenRouter standard prices + provenance) with an "accurate-or-null" policy replaced silently-$0 estimates; analyzer and runner now both recompute an agent-only cost from it (stored == recompute, parity-tested), fixing the implausible "opus cheaper than deepseek" ordering. The TimeSaved/ConversationSummary/sessionCoaching/memoryUpdate evals were bound to the production use-case-client contract (instead of drifted hand-mirrored copies), capped by an always-on AST drift guard. - [260604_2231] [Developer-facing] Sentry Autopilot CE2 wrapper—a thin overlay lets Sentry Autopilot route to CHIEF_ENGINEER2 in Light mode while preserving a zero-diff fallback to CHIEF_BUGFIXER, `runner.cli` is now injected into every `outcome.json` (so dual-runner A/B analysis works), and the base prompt was neutralised of CHIEF_BUGFIXER references for workflow-agnostic operation. - [260604_2156] [Developer-facing] Provider-routing SSOT rearchitecture—plan-mode targeting moved from a model-string sentinel to a typed plan-mode target, preflight became a discriminated result (`client | proxy-required | unavailable`), and the route decision is now materialised once per request (killing a double-derive). A typed model-eligibility authority was added as a pure view over that single route decision (additive—not yet wired into production consumers), alongside a dormant layer (provider-eligibility mirror, ordered-list types, single reasoning-effort resolver) and a planning-sentinel lint guard that lock in the new shape. No user-visible behaviour change. Commits ac972b417, 8a4be2dd1, 829cf2dea, 2595b11f4, 27078aa64, 373664d3e, 87696ab44, 829441d7a, 33a590b58, 7d0f6f1a3, 8afee2d7b, 8262bebd1, d6bde7e18. (Team Member)

The canonical judge panel is now the hard default (non-canonical is an explicit opt-in gate), incomplete-agent runs recover end-to-end, and additive reproduction + why-it-failed telemetry was added score-safely. - [260604_1716] [Developer-facing][Important] Submodule-pin-orphan prevention—a by-construction pin-ancestry gate now blocks a git-safe-sync push (exit 19) when a submodule's recorded pin has diverged from—or is merely ahead of—its `.gitmodules` tracked branch (fail-open only when the pin can't be verified, e.g. a transient fetch failure → rerun). The submodule-pointer smell test is tied to this gate, and super-mcp's realpath symlink defense-in-depth (lost in the pin rollback that orphaned bulk_export) was restored. This catches the verifiable orphan-prone pins—the class that silently dropped bulk_export—before the superproject push. ## [0.4.44] — 2026-06-02

### Changed
- [260530_2012] [User-facing][Important] Default model—Claude Opus 4.8 (released 2026-05-28) is now the default planning/thinking model across the Anthropic-subscription, pay-as-you-go, and OpenRouter providers. Opus 4.7 and 4.6 stay user-selectable, and older deprecated Opus entries retarget their migration to 4.8. Pricing/context metadata matches Opus 4.7. Commit 422dd9111. (Team Member)

### Added
- [260602_0835] [User-facing][Important] Cloud-sync duplicate cleanup—Rebel now automatically detects Google Drive/Dropbox conflict-copy duplicates (`foo (1).md`, `(conflicted copy)`, nested chains) and offers a one-click, confirm-first tidy-up that moves only byte-identical copies into a dated quarantine folder (never deletes, atomic no-overwrite, rehash-guarded, symlink-safe). A standalone `cleanup-conflict-copies.ts` script (dry-run by default) and a user help doc let affected users clean up the pile that accumulated before the in-app fix. Commits 3ff31871d, 62bc07d3a, 8eaaba69f, 0798fce76, e51515494, 27d0d5181; rebel-system 18f7045. (Team Member)
- [260601_2210] [User-facing][Important] Approvals drawer—the approval card was redesigned from a cluttered two-disclosure-layer card into a calm trust row (destination · audience · reversibility) with a single "Review" entry point and risk-aware button hierarchy. Review now reveals full content for every sensitive approval type on demand (recovered locally), so the old inline preview / "content hidden for privacy" blocks are gone; credential-risk saves are promoted to high-risk styling instead of looking routine. Commits 1e878a5ad, 758f1acb9. (the team)
- [260601_1813] [User-facing][Important] Turn Usage tooltip—the tooltip now reads per-role model truth from a runtime-authored `roles[]` contract instead of string-comparing model ids, fixing the diagnosed bug where the planner rendered as two "Opus" rows and the Behind-the-Scenes model never appeared. Each row now shows friendly catalog labels (Planner / Main work / Behind the Scenes), per-model tokens and cost, and marks configured-but-unused models "(not used this turn)". Commits 17a8d55f8, 1a91fccc0, 1ee7b5146, 05828b60b, 5706613ec, 13be9b3e8, 1d9836c15, f97e96912. (Team Member)

### Fixed
- [260531_1511] [User-facing][Important] Turn liveness—conversations no longer stay stuck showing "still working" after they've actually finished, and a turn cut short by a crash or quit now derives an "Interrupted — answer may be incomplete" state with a one-tap Try again. Turn liveness is now a pure projection of the synced event log (single `deriveTurnLiveness` source) with the persisted `isBusy`/`activeTurnId` scalars demoted to a recomputed cache stamped at one persistence choke point, structurally eliminating the recurring stuck-`isBusy` bug family behind 7+ postmortems. Commits aa0b4c38e, 769e9f4b8, 5abf91373, 8246e297e, 9eda2c1ff, 10309285d, c3dbcb2f6; rebel-system 02a1fcb. (Team Member)
- [260530_2301] [User-facing][Important] Safety degradation—when the safety evaluator's infrastructure is unavailable, memory-write paths now fail closed by staging an `eval_error` for later review (closing the last silent-drop gap), and Rebel surfaces a "suggest a fallback model" degradation nudge so a degraded evaluator route is visible rather than silently denying. A fallback evaluator hop on a different model/transport was also added, with automation denial bookkeeping restored and honest no-human copy. Commits 7f4ea4b90, ec19f0526, c301379e7, d776a4e06, f72f6db3c. (Team Member)
- [260601_1700] [User-facing][Important] Cloud-sync conflict fan-out—conflict-copy files are now excluded from workspace sync so Drive/Dropbox conflict duplicates stop multiplying across machines, and cloud-service `deleteFile` is idempotent for already-missing files. Closes REBEL-62A / FOX-3447. Commits 0c319ffc7, 1f2ed4f26, 8c35b0790. (Team Member)
- [260531_2150] [User-facing][Important] Long-turn responsiveness—conversation-shape derivation is now O(n) instead of O(n²), stopping the beachball on very long conversations, and transient `thinking_delta` events are no longer persisted across any of the five session paths. Commits f7a63cdaf, e2ba06b76. (Team Member)
- [260531_1632] [User-facing][Important] Meeting transcripts—failed-transcript recovery now actually re-saves on relaunch (the 24h retry cap and a pre-auth startup race had been silently defeating recovery for older transcripts), and the dedup walker is hardened against stray non-directory entries that previously threw mid-scan and lost recorded meeting transcripts. Commits affcc42a0, e34fa46aa. (Team Member)
- [260531_2237] [User-facing] Cloud self-update—fixed a SHA-abbreviation-length mismatch that produced `MANIFEST_UNKNOWN` failures once the repo's short git abbreviation grew past 7 characters. Commit 9fbbd0d82. (Team Member)
- [260530_2055] [User-facing][Important] Cloud capacity—cloud tool-index warmup no longer OOMs on the 4 GB Fly machine: embeddings are generated in batches instead of one ~4.4 GB attention buffer for the whole tool catalog. Closes REBEL-5ZS. Commit f7e516603. (Team Member)
- [260531_0850] [User-facing] Provider/onboarding—Mindstone managed-provider auto-select now respects a deliberate opt-out, OpenAI reasoning models no longer send an unsupported `temperature` (and non-reasoning models stop sending `reasoning_effort`) on the Chat-Completions proxy hop. Commits a7d43b593, 4d03e9a55, bc6b130bf, 3b3802290. (Team Member)
- [260531_1249] [User-facing][Important] Recovery messaging / REBEL-5BM—a turn whose recovery compaction succeeded but whose retry then hit a transient provider/connection error no longer shows the misleading "this conversation is still too large / fresh start" overlay. The exhaustion reason is now subtyped (so it stops being mislabeled `summary_generation_failed`), the real underlying error is attached to Sentry instead of being dropped by an `instanceof Error` gate, and the overlay copy is an allow-list that defaults safely for unmapped reasons. Commits d631a9046, 48a8d2d7b, d3e5bee20, fb64c463b, d4ffa4fea. (Team Member)
- [260531_1102] [Developer-facing] Sentry noise—deduped two recurring Sentry clusters: JSON-incompatible BTS-profile bypass info-events (~3799/72h, REBEL-5PN, where the fallback to the default auxiliary model works correctly) now dedupe while keeping per-occurrence ledger entries, and cloud warmup's expected dependency-unavailable condition (Super-MCP not started) is no longer reported as a generic exception while genuine Super-MCP startup failures stay visible to cloud Sentry (REBEL-5ZR). Commits 310a3a73f, 3cd3454c8. (Team Member)

### Fixed
- [260530_2002] [Developer-facing] Model capability drift guard—moved compact/max-effort/extended-context capability decisions onto `MODEL_CATALOG` flags for rostered Anthropic models with behavior-preserving fallback for unrostered ids, added invariant locks across model-id variants, and added an optional live `check:model-capabilities` script. No user-visible behavior change for currently rostered models. (Codex)
- [260530_1615] [Developer-facing] MCP telemetry / REBEL-13Y—`reportMcpError` now supports explicit fingerprint discriminators so execute/list MCP failures can group by structural kind+code instead of collapsing into one catch-all issue, and `onMcpError` now suppresses expected locally-cancelled MCP requests (`requestSignalAborted === true`) while still reporting AbortError-shaped upstream timeouts. No user-visible behavior changed. (Codex)
- [260530_0045] [Developer-facing][Important] Anthropic compaction / REBEL-52B—context-management requests that include the `compact_20260112` edit now also send `anthropic-beta: compact-2026-01-12` (deduplicated with stable ordering alongside `context-management-2025-06-27`), compact rejection fallback detection is now structural/token-anchored instead of prose-anchored, non-Anthropic OpenRouter proxy rewrites strip both Anthropic-only beta flags, and compact capability gating now has one shared source of truth. The OSS package adds: graceful unconfigured mode (no more `process.exit(1)` when key missing — server returns structured `NOT_CONFIGURED` per call), structured `{ok, code, error, resolution}` recovery contract across 8 error codes, sanitisation of API keys/prompts/paths from logs and error payloads, configurable `OPENAI_IMAGE_REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS` (default 90s) composed with caller AbortSignal via `AbortSignal.any()`, `destructiveHint`/`openWorldHint`/`idempotentHint` annotations, realpath fence on `edit_image` input paths, one-time symlink-safe `RebelImages/` → `MCP-Generated-Images/` folder migration. Host-side: removed OpenAI-specific lifecycle code in `coreStartup.ts`/`bundledInboxBridge.ts`/`settingsHandlers.ts`; replaced with generic `findRebelOssConnectorsUsingProviderKey` rotation handler so future Tier-3 ports inherit. Cloud-side: new `mcpEnvResolver` + `setPreRestartHook` re-resolves `providerKeys.openai` at every super-mcp spawn/restart. § 13 pre-publish security review skeleton committed at `docs-private/reports/security-reviews/260503_openai-image_0.1.0.md` with live-API probe evidence (real generate_image, 710 KB PNG, ~$0.04) and packed-tarball internal-reference scan (zero MINDSTONE_REBEL_BRIDGE_STATE / MCP_HOST_BRIDGE_STATE / REBEL_WORKSPACE_PATH matches). Upstream PR: https://github.com/mindstone/mcp-servers/pull/37. Plan: `docs/plans/260503_openai_image_oss_migration.md`. Commits 1d1ddfa56, 559cf1682, f1758920e, 536ac54b0, 00abfae8f. (Droid)

### Added
- [260511_1230] [Developer-facing][Important] Secret scanning—TruffleHog wired in as the primary secret detector, replacing Droid Shield for this repo. Pre-commit hook (`.husky/pre-commit`) hard-fails if `trufflehog` is not installed and blocks any commit containing a verified live credential. New CI workflow (`.github/workflows/secret-scan.yml`) runs the same `--results=verified --fail` scan on every push to `dev`/`main` and all PRs. Dev setup script (`scripts/setup-dev-mac.sh`) auto-installs TruffleHog via Homebrew. Bypass via `SKIP_TRUFFLEHOG=1` for genuine emergencies. Verification mode dramatically reduces false positives on AI-generated example keys. See `docs/project/SECRET_SCANNING.md`. (Droid)

- [260424_1113] [Developer-facing] super-mcp—`/stats` endpoint with per-package lifecycle counters. Exposes router metadata (pid, uptime, start_count, restart_count) and per-child stats (pid, connected, idle_ms, spawn/reap/eviction counts) as JSON for Rebel-side perf diagnostic consumption. - [260423_2228] [Developer-facing] Evals harness—cost/quality analyzer overhaul: cost-per-confidence-point metric, Pareto-frontier decision view on cost vs confidence, per-family cost/quality breakdown table. Aggregates use ratio-of-means (not mean-of-ratios) on pair-filtered runs, priceUnknown sentinels propagate through `Promise.allSettled`, arbitrator-only panels fail fast at startup, and a reusable `assertArbitratorInvariants` helper pins runtime behaviour. Commits 643c826b9, 8b33ef94f, 8ee7aefe5, a8d9dc9a0, bbc04e6ab, f1e32862c, 2686158a2, a2493ff2f. (Team Member)
- OpenAI Image Generation MCP upgraded to `gpt-image-2` (launched 2026-04-21). Sharper text rendering (including multilingual non-Latin scripts), better realism, new `moderation` parameter (`auto`/`low`), optional per-process `REBEL_OPENAI_IMAGE_MODEL` env-var rollback seam for operator emergencies. Default `quality` changed from `auto` to `high` to match the new model's strengths (per-image price at 1024² is cheaper at low/medium but ~60% more expensive at high — billed direct to the user's OpenAI account, not Rebel). `403 Forbidden` responses now map to org-verification guidance. Stage 3d adds `edit_image`, which calls `/v1/images/edits` with 1–4 reference images plus an optional PNG mask; edits typically cost ~$0.25–$0.40 at square/high because the references are billed at high-fidelity input rate. Catalog description + user-facing help + `OPENAI_IMAGE_MCP.md` refreshed; `bundledInboxBridge.ts` hot re-registration means no restart needed when adding the OpenAI key. Planning doc: `docs/plans/260422_gpt_image_2_enable.md`
- Rebel Browser install-delight flow (Stage 10-preview). New "Install Rebel Browser" CTA in Settings → Connectors seeds a conversation via `setupPromptGenerator` that calls `rebel_bridge_list_browsers`, asks the user which browser to use, and walks them through the Developer-Mode install. The Settings panel now detects installed Chromium browsers (Chrome, Edge, Brave, Arc, Vivaldi, Opera) and exposes a per-browser "Prepare install" button that extracts → reveals → opens the extensions page in one click. TOFU approval cards surface new extension IDs the first time they connect; Approve/Reject round-trips through the origin guard with a 120 s TTL. Planning doc: `docs/plans/finished/260419_rebel_browser_install_delight.md`
- Native Messaging Host (NMH) manifests land on disk (latent) alongside each pair so a future release can flip the extension's transport off the WS socket without rerunning the installer. Relay binary is not bundled yet; the manifest content points at a stable `<userData>/appBridge/bin/` placeholder. Hardened per security review F9: realpath ancestry check, atomic `wx`+chmod 0o600+rename write, host-name allowlist on unregister. Windows `reg add` / `reg delete` for the HKCU entry. IPC: `app-bridge:register-nmh` / `app-bridge:unregister-nmh`
- Rebel Browser Extension shipped to all users via Settings → Connectors (previously dev-gated). Pairs with the local App Bridge over a 6-digit code, then lets Rebel read, fill, and click in the tab you're looking at — without leaving your machine
- Stage 9 of the App Bridge plan: full release readiness — 8 deterministic Playwright scenarios (`npm run test:e2e:bridge-browser`), safety-fixtures regression test (`npm run eval:app-bridge-safety`), docs, UI polish, and catalog visibility flip
- Mobile offline queue now survives auth expiry without losing user data (queued items resume after re-sign-in on same cloud)
- Mobile offline attachments now queue and send when reconnected (previously silently dropped)
- Queue status banner shows clear state: offline, reconnecting, auth expired, draining, failures; separate toast appears when queue size limit is reached
- Per-conversation "Queued (N)" badge in conversation list
- Animated queued message chip (waiting → sending → done/failed) on conversation transcript

### Security
- App Bridge extension enforces sensitive-field / destructive-click policy at the extension boundary — bridge forwards commands unchanged, extension refuses password / OTP / payment fills without explicit per-field approval and refuses Delete / Pay / Cancel clicks without per-action approval. Covered by safety fixtures 154-157 (nightly eval) and `tests/e2e/app-bridge/fill-form-safety-reject.spec.ts` + `click-destructive-reject.spec.ts`
- Pair tokens are strictly single-scope (WS only) — any attempt to use them against `/apps/*` is rejected with 403 and a Sentry breadcrumb. Verified by `token-revoke.spec.ts`

Sensitive fields (passwords, OTP, payment) and destructive clicks (Delete / Pay / Cancel) still require explicit approval per action — no silent keystrokes. The bridge binds a local port, autostarts with Rebel, and falls back gracefully if the default port is taken. Stage 9 of the App Bridge plan. Plan: `docs/plans/260418_rebel_app_bridge_and_browser_extension.md`. (Droid)
- [260418_2000] [Developer-facing] App Bridge—Stage 9 release readiness. 8 deterministic Playwright scenarios (`npm run test:e2e:bridge-browser`, ~875ms), safety-fixtures regression test (`npm run eval:app-bridge-safety`), `docs/project/APP_BRIDGE.md`, `rebel-system/help-for-humans/browser-extension.md`, new `app-bridge:restart-dynamic-port` IPC for the port-conflict CTA, and catalog visibility flip (`hidden: true → false`). Extension build produces `dist/browser-extension.zip` via `npm run build:browser-extension`. (Droid)
- [260418_1200] [User-facing][Important] Library—comments on markdown files now clear when the message actually dispatches to Rebel, not when you click Send. Fixes the user-reported bug where annotations stayed on the file after Send to Rebel and visibly reanchored when Rebel edited the file. Clear fires from a per-message `onCommit` callback on `QueuedMessage` that runs after `processMessage` resolves; App.tsx accumulates callbacks per session and drops them on session delete, draft discard, or composer-empty transition so stale clears can never fire on the wrong submit. (Droid)
- [260418_1200] [User-facing] Settings—restore add-account button for manual-setup connectors and flash scrollbar on expand. Expanded connector card now scrolls to the setup form when users click Add account. (Team Member)
- [260418_1200] [Developer-facing] Annotations—centralize shared formatter in `packages/shared/src/annotationUtils.ts` with prompt-injection hardening. `generateAnnotationId` + `formatAnnotationMessage` + `buildAnnotationMessageSafe` (3× nonce retry, throws `AnnotationFormatExhaustionError` on exhaustion — no silent fallback) shared by document + conversation annotation surfaces. Trusted prologue sits OUTSIDE the fence; untrusted text is fence-sealed with a 128-bit nonce, UTF-8-safe truncated, and sanitised for control chars. Call sites (DocumentFooter, AnnotationOrchestrator) catch exhaustion, log, toast, and abort the send. Trim standardised to 100 chars (was 80). Plan: `docs/plans/260417_centralize_annotations_and_fix_document_send_clear.md`. (Droid)
- [260418_1200] [Developer-facing] Message queue—per-message `onCommit?: () => void | Promise<void>` on `QueuedMessage`. Fires exactly once after dispatch resolves successfully in both immediate-send and queued-flush paths; never fires on removal, rejection, or session delete. Async rejections are caught and logged (error-level, structured) so a misbehaving cleanup hook cannot break the queue. See `docs/project/ARCHITECTURE_MESSAGE_QUEUE.md § Per-message onCommit`. (Droid)

All 14 matrix rows from the planning doc now have explicit coverage. (Droid)

- [260418_0400] [User-facing] Mobile—drafts survive send failures on every entry point.
